{"parentUuid":"5c9c94f6-efd4-4cd6-aa0f-009937201e8b","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"dfb178e0-4750-4e30-89d2-a96d8e042d19","agentId":"a78bdc2b5817029ed","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01WevhBhbuUvmTraxjFzBsSd","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# ep2-crypto: 5-Minute BTC Prediction Engine\n     2→\n     3→## Project Overview\n     4→\n     5→ep2-crypto is a multi-edge Bitcoin price prediction system targeting 5-minute directional forecasts on BTC/USDT perpetual futures. It combines order flow microstructure, cross-market lead-lag, regime-adaptive modeling, and confidence gating to achieve a tradeable edge.\n     6→\n     7→**Realistic expectations** (from 500K+ words of research):\n     8→- Directional accuracy: 52-56% at 5-min horizon\n     9→- Backtest-to-live Sharpe degradation: 50-70% (need Sharpe >2.0 in backtest to survive)\n    10→- Round-trip costs: 8-12 bps minimum\n    11→- Alpha half-life: 1-6 months for ML patterns\n    12→- Optimal feature count: 18-25 (not 200+)\n    13→\n    14→## Tech Stack\n    15→\n    16→| Component | Choice | Why |\n    17→|-----------|--------|-----|\n    18→| Language | Python 3.12+ | ML ecosystem, async support |\n    19→| Package manager | uv | Fast, deterministic (never pip/poetry) |\n    20→| Primary model | LightGBM | Outperforms XGBoost by 0.5-1.5% on 5-min crypto |\n    21→| Secondary model | CatBoost | Ordered boosting prevents leakage, adds diversity |\n    22→| Sequence model | GRU (PyTorch) | Hidden state extracted as features for LightGBM |\n    23→| Ensemble | Stacking (logistic regression meta-learner) | 2-5% over best single model |\n    24→| Regime detection | Hierarchical (HMM + BOCPD + GARCH + Efficiency Ratio) | Faster detection than HMM alone |\n    25→| Exchange data | ccxt (WebSocket + REST) | Binance WS for klines/depth/trades, Bybit for derivatives |\n    26→| Cross-market | yfinance, Twelve Data | NQ, Gold, DXY (15-min delayed, acceptable) |\n    27→| On-chain | mempool.space WS | Whale detection only (on-chain operates at 4h+, not 5-min) |\n    28→| Logging | structlog | Structured JSON logs, never print() |\n    29→| API | FastAPI + uvicorn | Prediction endpoints, health, metrics |\n    30→| Database | SQLite (dev) -> TimescaleDB (prod) | Zero setup for dev |\n    31→| Inference | ONNX Runtime | 2-5x speedup over native |\n    32→| Tuning | Optuna | MedianPruner, Sharpe objective |\n    33→| Testing | pytest + pytest-cov | Required for every feature computation |\n    34→| Linting | ruff + mypy (strict) | Type safety, code quality |\n    35→\n    36→## Key Architecture Decisions\n    37→\n    38→These decisions are the result of extensive research (49 files in `research/`). Do NOT change them without reviewing the corresponding ADR in `DECISIONS.md`.\n    39→\n    40→### Model Architecture\n    41→- **LightGBM over XGBoost** (ADR-001): Faster training, better accuracy on crypto tick data\n    42→- **Stacking ensemble over per-regime models** (ADR-006): Per-regime models fragment scarce data. Single ensemble with regime as input feature is more robust\n    43→- **Ternary target (up/flat/down) with adaptive threshold** (ADR-002): Acknowledges untradeable low-volatility periods. Threshold adapts per regime\n    44→- **Triple barrier labeling over fixed threshold** (ADR-008): Accounts for time decay and stop-loss, produces more realistic labels\n    45→\n    46→### Data & Features\n    47→- **Dual normalization pipeline** (ADR in RESEARCH_SYNTHESIS.md): Raw features for tree models (normalization harms trees), robust scaling + rank-to-gaussian for neural models\n    48→- **On-chain as regime context only, not primary signal** (ADR-004): On-chain signals operate at 4h-24h, not 5-min\n    49→- **Skip real-time sentiment, use funding rate** (ADR-005): NLP sentiment too slow for 5-min. Funding rate is the only useful \"sentiment\" at this timeframe\n    50→- **Feature priority**: Microstructure (OBI, OFI, microprice) captures 60-80% of achievable 5-min signal\n    51→\n    52→### Validation & Risk\n    53→- **Purged walk-forward validation**: 14-day sliding window, 18-bar purge (90 min), 12-bar embargo (60 min). Sliding, NOT expanding (crypto non-stationarity)\n    54→- **Confidence gating pipeline**: isotonic calibration -> meta-labeling -> conformal prediction -> adaptive threshold -> drawdown gate. This is the single biggest Sharpe multiplier (2-4x)\n    55→- **Quarter-Kelly position sizing**: Position size = 0.25 * Kelly fraction * confidence score\n    56→- **Annualization**: sqrt(105,120) for 24/7 crypto. 288 bars/day * 365 days = 105,120 bars/year. NEVER use sqrt(252)\n    57→\n    58→### Infrastructure\n    59→- **asyncio single-process architecture** (ADR-010): All collectors and processing in one event loop\n    60→- **Event-driven backtest engine with Numba** (ADR-009): 100x faster than pure Python, realistic fills\n    61→- **Numpy ring buffers** for data structures: 10-20x less memory than pandas DataFrames on hot path\n    62→\n    63→## Code Conventions\n    64→\n    65→### Mandatory Rules\n    66→1. **Named exports only** - never use `export default` or bare module-level assignments\n    67→2. **structlog for all logging** - never use `print()` for any output\n    68→3. **Parameterized SQL queries only** - never use f-strings or string interpolation for SQL\n    69→4. **All features must use only past data** - no look-ahead bias. Every feature computation at time t may only use data from times <= t\n    70→5. **Type hints on all functions** - mypy strict mode is enforced\n    71→6. **Tests required for every feature computation** - including golden dataset tests against hand-verified values\n    72→7. **No `any` types** - be explicit with all type annotations\n    73→8. **No TODO/FIXME/HACK without linked issue** - if you must leave one, create a GitHub issue first\n    74→9. **Secrets via environment variables** - never commit API keys, never use .env files in repo\n    75→\n    76→### Error Handling\n    77→- Always use try/catch with meaningful error messages at system boundaries\n    78→- Never swallow errors silently - log with context via structlog\n    79→- Never fire-and-forget async operations - track completion\n    80→- Health endpoints must check actual dependencies, not just return \"ok\"\n    81→\n    82→### Feature Engineering Rules\n    83→- Every feature must be tested for look-ahead bias (shuffle test + truncation test)\n    84→- Rolling calculations use only past data (no centered windows)\n    85→- NaN handling: forward-fill for price data, zero for counts, drop for model input\n    86→- All normalization fitted on training data only, per fold\n    87→\n    88→### Commit Hygiene\n    89→- Meaningful commit messages explaining WHY, not just WHAT\n    90→- Pass lint + typecheck + test before committing\n    91→- One logical change per commit, max 5 commits per feature\n    92→- Build one feature, verify, commit - never batch 5 features\n    93→\n    94→## Project Structure\n    95→\n    96→```\n    97→ep2-crypto/\n    98→├── CLAUDE.md                    # THIS FILE - project context for AI sessions\n    99→├── PLAN.md                      # Original development plan (Phase 0-11)\n   100→├── RESEARCH_SYNTHESIS.md        # Distilled findings from 49 research files\n   101→├── BACKTESTING_PLAN.md          # Comprehensive backtesting methodology\n   102→├── SPRINTS.md                   # Sprint planning with acceptance criteria\n   103→├── REQUIREMENTS.md              # Functional and non-functional requirements\n   104→├── DECISIONS.md                 # Architecture Decision Records (ADR-001 to ADR-010)\n   105→├── pyproject.toml               # Dependencies and tool configuration\n   106→├── uv.lock                      # Locked dependencies\n   107→├── research/                    # 49 research files (read-only reference)\n   108→│   ├── meta_labeling_deep_research.md\n   109→│   ├── microstructure_ofi_microprice.md\n   110→│   ├── monte_carlo_validation.md\n   111→│   ├── retraining_strategies.md\n   112→│   ├── statistical_validation_tests.py\n   113→│   ├── STRESS_TESTING.md\n   114→│   ├── transaction_cost_modeling.md\n   115→│   └── ... (42 more research files)\n   116→├── src/\n   117→│   └── ep2_crypto/\n   118→│       ├── __init__.py\n   119→│       ├── config.py                  # Pydantic Settings, env-var based\n   120→│       ├── db/\n   121→│       │   ├── schema.py              # SQLite/TimescaleDB schema\n   122→│       │   └── repository.py          # Parameterized query layer\n   123→│       ├── ingest/\n   124→│       │   ├── base.py                # Base collector interface\n   125→│       │   ├── exchange.py            # Binance WS: klines, depth@100ms, aggTrades\n   126→│       │   ├── derivatives.py         # Bybit: OI, funding, liquidations\n   127→│       │   ├── onchain.py             # mempool.space: whale detection\n   128→│       │   ├── cross_market.py        # NQ, Gold, DXY, ETH\n   129→│       │   ├── macro.py               # Economic calendar, event monitoring\n   130→│       │   └── orchestrator.py        # Async task management, reconnection\n   131→│       ├── features/\n   132→│       │   ├── base.py                # Feature pipeline interface\n   133→│       │   ├── microstructure.py      # OBI, OFI, microprice, spread, TFI\n   134→│       │   ├── volume.py              # Volume delta, VWAP deviation, rate-of-change\n   135→│       │   ├── volatility.py          # Realized, Parkinson, EWMA, vol-of-vol\n   136→│       │   ├── momentum.py            # ROC, RSI, linreg slope, quantile rank\n   137→│       │   ├── cross_market.py        # Lead-lag, correlation, divergence\n   138→│       │   ├── temporal.py            # Cyclical encoding, session, time-to-funding\n   139→│       │   ├── regime_features.py     # ER, GARCH vol, HMM probs as features\n   140→│       │   ├── normalization.py       # Dual pipeline (raw for trees, robust for neural)\n   141→│       │   └── pipeline.py            # Combines all feature sets\n   142→│       ├── regime/\n   143→│       │   ├── detector.py            # Hierarchical regime detection\n   144→│       │   ├── hmm.py                 # 2-state GaussianHMM\n   145→│       │   ├── bocpd.py               # Bayesian Online Change Point Detection\n   146→│       │   ├── garch.py               # GJR-GARCH(1,1)-t conditional volatility\n   147→│       │   └── efficiency_ratio.py    # Kaufman Efficiency Ratio\n   148→│       ├── models/\n   149→│       │   ├── lgbm_direction.py      # LightGBM ternary classifier\n   150→│       │   ├── catboost_direction.py  # CatBoost ternary classifier\n   151→│       │   ├── gru_features.py        # GRU hidden state extractor\n   152→│       │   ├── quantile.py            # LightGBM quantile regression (5 quantiles)\n   153→│       │   ├── stacking.py            # Logistic regression meta-learner\n   154→│       │   ├── calibration.py         # Isotonic regression calibration\n   155→│       │   └── tuning.py              # Optuna hyperparameter optimization\n   156→│       ├── confidence/\n   157→│       │   ├── meta_labeling.py       # Meta-labeling gate\n   158→│       │   ├── conformal.py           # Conformal prediction gate\n   159→│       │   ├── gating.py              # Full confidence gating pipeline\n   160→│       │   └── position_sizing.py     # Quarter-Kelly sizing\n   161→│       ├── backtest/\n   162→│       │   ├── walk_forward.py        # Purged walk-forward with embargo\n   163→│       │   ├── engine.py              # Event-driven backtest engine  211→\n   212→# Verify installation\n   213→uv run python -c \"import ep2_crypto\"\n   214→```\n   215→\n   216→### Tests\n   217→```bash\n   218→# Run all tests\n   219→uv run pytest\n   220→\n   221→# Run with coverage\n   222→uv run pytest --cov=ep2_crypto --cov-report=term-missing\n   223→\n   224→# Run specific test module\n   225→uv run pytest tests/test_features/\n   226→```\n   227→\n   228→### Linting and Type Checking\n   229→```bash\n   230→# Lint\n   231→uv run ruff check src/ tests/\n   232→\n   233→# Format\n   234→uv run ruff format src/ tests/\n   235→\n   236→# Type check\n   237→uv run mypy src/ep2_crypto/\n   238→```\n   239→\n   240→### Data Collection\n   241→```bash\n   242→# Backfill historical data (60 days OHLCV, OI, funding)\n   243→uv run python scripts/collect_history.py\n   244→\n   245→# Start live data collection\n   246→uv run python scripts/live.py --collect-only\n   247→```\n   248→\n   249→### Training\n   250→```bash\n   251→# Full training pipeline (walk-forward)\n   252→uv run python scripts/train.py\n   253→\n   254→# Hyperparameter tuning\n   255→uv run python scripts/train.py --tune --trials 100\n   256→```\n   257→\n python scripts/backtest.py --start 2025-01-01 --end 2025-03-01\n   265→```\n   266→\n   267→### API Server\n   268→```bash\n   269→# Start prediction API\n   270→uv run uvicorn Each sprint has:\n   276→- Clear objectives and deliverables\n   277→- Acceptance criteria that must pass before moving on\n   278→- Key files to create/modify\n   279→- Dependencies on previous sprints\n   280→\n   281→**Current sprint progress**: See `SPRINTS.md` for status.\n   282→\n   283→## Key Research References\n   284→\n   285→When implementing a module, consult the relevant research files in `research/`:\n   286→\n   287→| Module | Key Research Files |\n   288→|--------|-------------------|\n   289→| Microstructure features | `microstructure_ofi_microprice.md` |\n   290→| Meta-labeling | `meta_labeling_deep_research.md` |\n   291→| Monte Carlo validation | `monte_carlo_validation.md` |\n   292→| Stress testing | `STRESS_TESTING.md` |\n   293→| Transaction costs | `transaction_cost_modeling.md` |\n   294→| Model retraining | `retraining_strategies.md` |\n   295→| Statistical validation | `statistical_validation_tests.py` (executable code) |\n   296→| Full synthesis | `RESEARCH_SYNTHESIS.md` (root) |\n   297→| Backtesting methodology | `BACKTESTING_PLAN.md` (root) |\n   298→| Architecture decisions | `DECISIONS.md` (root) |\n   299→\n   300→## Risk Parameters (Starting Configuration)\n   301→\n   302→| Parameter | Value |\n   303→|-----------|-------|\n   304→| Position size per trade | 4-5% of capital (quarter-Kelly capped) |\n   305→| Daily loss limit | 2-3% of capital |\n   306→| Weekly loss limit | 5% of capital |\n   307→| Max drawdown halt | 15% of capital |\n   308→| Catastrophic stop per trade | 3 ATR |\n   309→| Max open positions | 1 |\n   310→| Max trades per day | 30 |\n   311→| Trading hours | 08:00-21:00 UTC (Europe + US sessions) |\n   312→| Weekend position sizing | -30% reduction |\n   313→| Confidence threshold | 0.60 (starting, adaptive) |\n   314→| Min bar volatility | 15% annualized |\n   315→| Max bar volatility | 150% annualized |\n   316→\n   317→## Critical Numbers\n   318→\n   319→| Parameter | Value |\n   320→|-----------|-------|\n   321→| Annualization factor | sqrt(105,120) = 324.22 (NOT sqrt(252)) |\n   322→| Bars per year | 288/day * 365 = 105,120 |\n   323→| Training window | 14 days (4,032 bars) sliding |\n   324→| Test window | 1 day (288 bars) |\n   325→| Purge size | 18 bars (90 min) |\n   326→| Embargo size | 12 bars (60 min) |\n   327→| Target backtest Sharpe | > 2.0 (to survive 50-70% degradation) |\n   328→| Break-even cost target | Strategy must survive > 15 bps round-trip |\n   329→| Expected live Sharpe | 0.6-1.0 (after degradation) |\n   330→| Round-trip cost assumption | 8-12 bps (conservative) |\n   331→\n   332→## Anti-Patterns to Avoid\n   333→\n   334→1. Never random-split time series data\n   335→2. Never use `bidirectional=True` on GRU (uses future data)\n   336→3. Never use centered rolling windows for features (look-ahead bias)\n   337→4. Never trust >70% directional accuracy without checking for look-ahead bias\n   338→5. Never use SMOTE or other oversampling on time series\n   339→6. Never interpolate missing data (forward-fill or drop only)\n   340→7. Never use global normalization (fit on all data) - always per-fold on training data\n   341→8. Never use expanding window for training - crypto non-stationarity makes old data harmful\n   342→9. Never skip transaction costs in backtest evaluation\n   343→10. Never commit without lint + typecheck + test passing\n   344→\n   345→## Research Reference\n   346→\n   347→All research is in `research/` with `research/INDEX.md` as the master lookup.\n   348→Files follow `RR-{category}-{topic}.md` naming. Key files per area:\n   349→\n   350→| Need to implement... | Read this first |\n   351→|---------------------|-----------------|\n   352→| WebSocket data ingestion | `RR-api-ccxt-exchange-integration.md` |\n   353→| Order book features (OBI, OFI) | `RR-ofi-microprice-implementation.md` |\n   354→| Liquidation cascade detection | `RR-cascade-liquidation-detection-system.md` |\n   355→| Cross-market NQ lead-lag | `RR-crossmarket-lead-lag-correlations.md` |\n   356→| Regime detection (HMM etc) | `RR-regime-detection-methods.md` |\n   357→| LightGBM training | `RR-lightgbm-crypto-tuning.md` |\n   358→| GRU/TCN architecture | `RR-gru-tcn-training-architecture.md` |\n   359→| Meta-labeling | `RR-metalabeling-implementation-guide.md` |\n   360→| Walk-forward validation | `RR-walkforward-validation-methods.md` |\n   361→| Backtesting framework | `RR-backtest-framework-design.md` |\n   362→| Statistical validation | `RR-stats-edge-vs-luck-tests.md` |\n   363→| Transaction costs | `RR-costs-transaction-cost-modeling.md` |\n   364→| Paper trading | `RR-papertrade-system-architecture.md` |\n   365→| Alpha decay monitoring | `RR-decay-edge-disappearance-detection.md` |\n   366→\n   367→## Pre-Code Checklists\n   368→\n   369→### Before writing ANY feature computation:\n   370→- [ ] Does it use ONLY data at times <= t? (no look-ahead)\n   371→- [ ] Is it tested with a truncation test? (compute on data[:150] matches data[:200] at index 150)\n   372→- [ ] Does it have a unit test with known input/output?\n   373→- [ ] Is it added to the golden dataset for regression testing?\n   374→- [ ] Is normalization rolling (not global)?\n   375→- [ ] For tree model path: raw value (no normalization)\n   376→- [ ] For neural model path: robust scaling or rank-to-gaussian\n   377→\n   378→### Before writing ANY model training code:\n   379→- [ ] Is the train/val/test split temporal (never random)?\n   380→- [ ] Is early stopping validation carved from training set (not test set)?\n   381→- [ ] Is there a purge gap (18 bars) between train and test?\n   382→- [ ] Is there an embargo (12 bars) after test?\n   383→- [ ] Are sample weights applied (time decay + regime balance)?\n   384→- [ ] Is the target ternary with adaptive threshold?\n   385→\n   386→### Before any backtest evaluation:\n   387→- [ ] Are transaction costs included (8-12 bps round-trip)?\n   388→- [ ] Is execution at next-bar-open (never current-bar-close)?\n   389→- [ ] Is latency simulated (200ms minimum)?\n   390→- [ ] Are funding rate costs modeled for positions held across settlement?\n   391→- [ ] Does the backtest period include at least one bull AND one bear market?\n   392→\n   393→## Session Management\n   394→\n   395→**CRITICAL: Read `PROGRESS.md` at the start of EVERY session.** It has:\n   396→- Current sprint and ticket\n   397→- What was done in previous sessions\n   398→- The EXACT next step to take\n   399→- Any handoff notes from the previous session\n   400→\n   401→Full protocol is in `SESSION_PROTOCOL.md`. Key rules:\n   402→1. One ticket per session is fine — quality over speed\n   403→2. Never read research files unless actively implementing from them (they're 10-50KB)\n   404→3. Update PROGRESS.md at end of session with what was done + exact next step\n   405→4. If context is getting large, wrap up — don't push through\n   406→\n   407→### End-of-Session Handover\n   408→\n   409→At the END of every session, you MUST:\n   410→1. Update PROGRESS.md (what was done, what wasn't, exact next step)\n   411→2. Commit code if any was written\n   412→3. **Generate a handover prompt** for the user to paste in the next session:\n   413→\n   414→```\n   415→Handover prompt for next session:\n   416→---\n   417→Read PROGRESS.md and continue from ticket S{X}-T{Y}. [1-sentence description of what's next].\n   418→Run verification after each ticket. Update PROGRESS.md before ending.\n   419→---\n   420→```\n   421→\n   422→### Sprint Completion Handover\n   423→\n   424→When a sprint is FULLY complete (all tickets `[x]`, acceptance criteria pass):\n   425→1. Commit with message `\"Sprint N complete: <summary>\"`\n   426→2. Decompose the next sprint into tickets in PROGRESS.md\n   427→3. **Generate the sprint handover prompt**:\n   428→\n   429→```\n   430→Sprint N COMPLETE. Start next session with:\n   431→---\n   432→Read PROGRESS.md and start Sprint {N+1}. The tickets are decomposed and ready.\n   433→Current ticket: S{N+1}-T1. Run verification after each ticket.\n   434→Update PROGRESS.md before ending.\n   435→---\n   436→```\n   437→\n   438→## Sprint Progress Tracking\n   439→\n   440→Current sprint status tracked in `SPRINTS.md` (high-level) and `PROGRESS.md` (ticket-level).\n   441→- `[ ]` = not started, `[~]` = in progress, `[x]` = complete\n   442→- Each ticket has verification commands — run them before marking complete\n   443→\n   444→## Data Sources (Complete)\n   445→\n   446→Primary: Binance WS (klines, depth, aggTrades), Bybit (OI, funding, liquidations), ccxt (ETH)\n   447→Cross-market: yfinance (NQ, Gold, DXY), Coinbase (premium), Deribit (options IV)\n   448→Alternative: mempool.space (whales), Alternative.me (Fear&Greed), **Polymarket** (BTC prediction markets)\n   449→Context only: on-chain metrics (4h+ timeframe, NOT 5-min signal)\n   450→"}]},"uuid":"99438c39-28d2-4f35-981e-c4e691b8a4f9","timestamp":"2026-03-23T13:50:19.505Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"5c9c94f6-efd4-4cd6-aa0f-009937201e8b","userType":"external","entrypoint":"claude-vscode","cwd":"/Users/edgarpocaterra/ep2-crypto","sessionId":"f48c9af0-2e30-4c92-9024-4c84a03f39db","version":"2.1.81","gitBranch":"main","slug":"spicy-gathering-plum"}

    1→# ep2-crypto: 5-Minute BTC Prediction Engine\n     2→\n     3→## Vision\n     4→A multi-edge Bitcoin price prediction system that combines on-chain signals, order flow microstructure, cross-market lead-lag, and regime-adaptive modeling — designed to be fundamentally different from the standard LSTM+RSI tutorial approach.\n     5→\n     6→---\n     7→\n     8→## Phase 0: Documentation Discovery (Completed)\n     9→\n    10→### Verified APIs & Libraries\n    11→\n    12→**Exchange Data (ccxt pro)**\n    13→- `watch_order_book(symbol, limit)` — real-time L2 order book (Binance supports limit=5,10,20,50)\n    14→- `watch_trades(symbol)` — aggTrade stream (sub-100ms latency)\n    15→- `watch_ohlcv(symbol, timeframe)` — kline streaming\n    16→- `fetch_open_interest(symbol)` / `fetch_funding_rate(symbol)` — Bybit derivatives (REST)\n    17→- Liquidations: NOT in ccxt — must use Bybit WebSocket directly (`allLiquidation.BTCUSDT`)\n    18→\n    19→**On-Chain Data (free, no auth)**\n    20→- mempool.space: REST + WebSocket (`wss://mempool.space/api/v1/ws`), `track-mempool` for streaming all new txs\n    21→- Blockchair: SQL-like filtering `?q=output_total(100000000..)` for whale detection (1,440 req/day free)\n    22→- blockchain.info: `/unconfirmed-transactions`, `/balance`, `/q/*` stats endpoints\n    23→- Alternative.me: Fear & Greed Index (`GET https://api.alternative.me/fng/`)\n    24→- Exchange inflow/outflow: NO free API exists — monitor known exchange addresses as workaround\n    25→\n    26→**Cross-Market Data**\n    27→- ETH: ccxt/Binance WebSocket (free, real-time, sub-100ms) — clear winner\n    28→- NQ/Gold/DXY historical: yfinance (`NQ=F`, `GC=F`, `DX-Y.NYB`) — 5-min bars, 15-min delayed, 60 days depth\n    29→- NQ/Gold near-real-time polling: Twelve Data (800 req/day free, `XAU/USD`)\n    30→- DXY: not available as native instrument anywhere free — must compute from forex components\n    31→\n    32→**ML Stack**\n    33→- XGBoost: `XGBClassifier`, incremental learning via `xgb_model=`, feature importance via `get_score(importance_type='gain')`\n    34→- PyTorch GRU: `nn.GRU(input_size, hidden_size, num_layers, batch_first=True)`, sequence length 12-60 steps\n    35→- HMM: `hmmlearn.GaussianHMM(n_components=3)`, no native online learning (use `init_params=\"\"` workaround)\n    36→- Optuna: `XGBoostPruningCallback` for XGB, `trial.report()`+`trial.should_prune()` for PyTorch\n    37→- Walk-forward: `sklearn.model_selection.TimeSeriesSplit(max_train_size=N)` for sliding window\n    38→- Feature engineering: `pandas-ta` (or `pandas-ta-classic` as fallback)\n    39→\n    40→### Anti-Patterns to Avoid\n    41→- Never random-split time series data\n    42→- Never use `bidirectional=True` on GRU (uses future data)\n    43→- Never run tsfresh in live prediction loop (offline feature discovery only)\n    44→- Never trust >70% directional accuracy without checking for look-ahead bias\n    45→- ccxt `binanceusdm` has intermittent WebSocket issues in v4.4.x — test your version\n    46→- Bybit order book via ccxt only supports depths [1, 50, 200, 1000] — slice from 50 for top-10\n    47→- hmmlearn is in maintenance mode — plan for potential migration\n    48→\n    49→---\n    50→\n    51→## Project Structure\n    52→\n    53→```\n    54→ep2-crypto/\n    55→├── Initialize Python project with uv, configure `pyproject.toml` with all dependencies\n   121→2. Set up SQLite database with schema for: OHLCV candles, order book snapshots, trades, on-chain events, cross-market prices, regime labels\n   122→3. Build parameterized query repository layer (no string interpolation)\n   123→4. Set up structlog logging configuration\n   124→5. Create `config.py` with environment-variable-based settings (no .env files committed)\n   125→\n   126→### Dependencies\n   127→```toml\n   128→[project]\n   129→requires-python = \">=3.12\"\n   130→dependencies = [\n   131→    \"ccxt>=4.4\",\n   132→    \"websockets>=13.0\",\n   133→    \"pandas>=2.2\",\n   134→    \"numpy>=2.0\",\n   135→    \"xgboost>=2.1\",\n   136→    \"torch>=2.5\",\n   137→    \"hmmlearn>=0.3\",\n   138→    \"optuna>=4.0\",\n   139→    \"pandas-ta>=0.3\",\n   140→    \"scikit-learn>=1.5\",\n   141→    \"fastapi>=0.115\",\n   142→    \"uvicorn>=0.32\",\n   143→    \"structlog>=24.0\",\n   144→    \"httpx>=0.27\",\n   145→    \"aiosqlite>=0.20\",\n   146→]\n   147→```\n   148→\n   149→### Verification\n   150→- [ ] `uv run python -c \"import ep2_crypto\"` works\n   151→- [ ] Database creates tables on first run\n   152→- [ ] All SQL uses parameterized queries (grep for f-strings in db/)\n   153→- [ ] structlog outputs JSON logs\n   154→\n   155→---\n   156→\n   157→## Phase 2: Data Ingestion — Exchange & Derivatives\n   158→\n   159→### What to implement\n   160→1. **Exchange collector** (`ingest/exchange.py`):\n   161→   - ccxt pro WebSocket: `watch_ohlcv('BTC/USDT:USDT', '1m')` for 1-min klines\n   162→   - ccxt pro WebSocket: `watch_order_book('BTC/USDT:USDT', limit=20)` for depth snapshots\n   163→   - ccxt pro WebSocket: `watch_trades('BTC/USDT:USDT')` for aggTrades\n   164→   - Store each to SQLite at configured intervals\n   165→\n   166→2. **Derivatives collector** (`ingest/derivatives.py`):\n   167→   - ccxt REST: `bybit.fetch_open_interest('BTC/USDT:USDT')` — poll every 5 min\n   168→   - ccxt REST: `bybit.fetch_funding_rate('BTC/USDT:USDT')` — poll every 5 min\n   169→   - Direct Bybit WebSocket: `allLiquidation.BTCUSDT` stream — real-time\n   170→   - Connection: `wss://stream.bybit.com/v5/public/linear`, subscribe `{\"op\":\"subscribe\",\"args\":[\"allLiquidation.BTCUSDT\"]}`\n   171→\n   172→3. **Orchestrator** (`ingest/orchestrator.py`):\n   173→   - Manages all collectors as async tasks\n   174→   - Handles reconnection, error logging, graceful shutdown\n   175→   - Health checks for each stream\n   176→\n   177→### Documentation references\n   178→- ccxt pro: `watch_order_book`, `watch_trades`, `watch_ohlcv` — batch_first pattern\n   179→- Bybit liquidation: `allLiquidation` topic (NOT deprecated `liquidation` topic)\n   180→- Bybit WS heartbeat: send `ping` every 20 seconds\n   181→\n   182→### Verification\n   183→- [ ] Run collectors for 10 minutes, verify data in SQLite\n   184→- [ ] Liquidation events appear when market is volatile\n   185→- [ ] OI and funding rate update every 5 minutes\n   186→- [ ] Reconnection works after simulated disconnect\n   187→- [ ] No duplicate records in database\n   188→\n   189→---\n   190→\n   191→## Phase 3: Data Ingestion — On-Chain & Cross-Market\n   192→\n   193→### What to implement\n   194→1. **On-chain collector** (`ingest/onchain.py`):\n   195→   - mempool.space WebSocket (`wss://mempool.space/api/v1/ws`):\n   196→     - Subscribe: `{\"action\":\"want\",\"data\":[\"blocks\",\"stats\"]}`\n   197→     - Subscribe: `{\"track-mempool\": true}` for all new txs\n   198→     - Client-side filter: flag transactions with output sum > 10 BTC as whale txs\n   199→   - Blockchair REST (polling every 60s):\n   200→     - `GET https://api.blockchair.com/bitcoin/mempool/transactions?q=output_total(1000000000..)&s=output_total(desc)`\n   201→     - Whale transactions > 10 BTC from mempool\n   202→   - Known exchange address monitoring:\n   203→     - Maintain a list of top 20 exchange cold/hot wallet addresses\n   204→     - Poll via mempool.space `/address/:address/txs` every 2 min\n   205→   - Alternative.me Fear & Greed: `GET https://api.alternative.me/fng/` — poll every 30 min\n   206→\n   207→2. **Cross-market collector** (`ingest/cross_market.py`):\n   208→   - ETH: ccxt pro `watch_ohlcv('ETH/USDT:USDT', '1m')` — real-time\n   209→   - NQ futures: yfinance `yf.download('NQ=F', interval='5m', period='5d')` — poll every 5 min\n   210→   - Gold: yfinance `yf.download('GC=F', interval='5m', period='5d')` — poll every 5 min\n   211→   - DXY: yfinance `yf.download('DX-Y.NYB', interval='5m', period='5d')` — poll every 5 min\n   212→   - Note: yfinance data is ~15 min delayed — acceptable for lead-lag detection (lag is minutes-to-hours)\n   213→\n   214→### Rate limit awareness\n   215→- Blockchair: max 30 req/min, 1,440/day — budget carefully\n   216→- mempool.space: no published limit, be respectful (1 WebSocket connection is fine)\n   217→- yfinance: no official limit, keep under 100 req/session\n   218→\n   219→### Verification\n   220→- [ ] Whale transactions detected and stored (check against whale-alert Twitter for validation)\n   221→- [ ] Mempool pressure metrics (size, fee rates) updating in real-time\n   222→- [ ] ETH price streaming alongside BTC\n   223→- [ ] NQ/Gold/DXY data updating every 5 min (with 15-min delay noted in metadata)\n   224→- [ ] Fear & Greed index stored with timestamps\n   225→\n   226→---\n   227→\n   228→## Phase 4: Feature Engineering — Microstructure Edge\n   229→\n   230→### What to implement\n   231→1. **Order book features** (`features/microstructure.py`):\n   232→   - Bid-ask spread: `(best_ask - best_bid) / mid_price`\n   233→   - Order book imbalance (top 5 levels): `(bid_vol - ask_vol) / (bid_vol + ask_vol)`\n   234→   - Depth imbalance: weighted by price proximity to mid\n   235→   - Book pressure: ratio of volume within 0.1% of mid on each side\n   236→   - Spread velocity: rate of change of spread over last N snapshots\n   237→\n   238→2. **Trade flow features** (`features/microstructure.py`):\n   239→   - Aggressive buy/sell ratio: classify trades by taker side from aggTrade `m` field (buyer is maker = sell aggression)\n   240→   - Trade intensity: trades per second, rolling 1-min and 5-min\n   241→   - Volume delta: cumulative (aggressive_buy_vol - aggressive_sell_vol)\n   242→   - Large trade detection: flag trades > 2 std devs above mean size\n   243→   - Trade clustering: count of trades in rapid succession (< 100ms apart)\n   244→\n   245→3. **Absorption detection** (`features/microstructure.py`):\n   246→   - Price doesn't move despite large aggressive orders hitting one side\n   247→   - Measure: large volume delta without proportional price change\n   248→   - Signal: potential hidden liquidity / institutional activity\n   249→\n   250→### Documentation references\n   251→- Binance aggTrade `m` field: `true` = buyer is market maker (i.e., trade was a sell aggression)\n   252→- Order book from `watch_order_book`: `ob['bids']` = [[price, amount], ...], `ob['asks']` = [[price, amount], ...]\n   253→\n   254→### Verification\n   255→- [ ] Order book imbalance correlates with short-term price direction (basic sanity check)\n   256→- [ ] Volume delta calculation matches manual spot-check\n   257→- [ ] Features update in real-time as new data arrives\n   258→- [ ] No look-ahead bias in feature calculations (features only use data available at calculation time)\n   259→\n   260→---\n   261→\n   262→## Phase 5: Feature Engineering — On-Chain & Cross-Market Edges\n   263→\n   264→### What to implement\n   265→1. **On-chain features** (`features/onchain.py`):\n   266→   - Whale flow score: net BTC moved to/from exchange addresses in rolling 30-min window\n   267→   - Mempool pressure: mempool size rate of change, fee spike detection\n   268→   - Large tx momentum: count and total value of >10 BTC transactions in last 15 min\n   269→   - Exchange balance delta: change in known exchange address balances (approximation)\n   270→   - Fear & Greed momentum: rate of change of index (not raw value — everyone has raw value)\n   271→\n   272→2. **Cross-market features** (`features/cross_market.py`):\n   273→   - Lead-lag correlation: rolling Pearson correlation between BTC returns and NQ/Gold/DXY returns at various lags (0, 1, 2, 5, 10 min)\n   274→   - Dynamic lead-lag detection: which asset is currently leading? Use Granger causality test on rolling window\n   275→   - Divergence signals: BTC moving opposite to its current leader = mean reversion signal\n   276→   - ETH/BTC ratio momentum: rate of change of ETH/BTC price ratio (risk appetite proxy)\n   277→   - Cross-market volatility spillover: when NQ vol spikes, does BTC vol follow? Rolling correlation of volatility\n   278→\n   279→3. **Temporal features** (`features/temporal.py`):\n   280→   - Cyclical encoding: `sin(2π × minute/60)`, `cos(2π × minute/60)` for minute-of-hour\n   281→   - Same for hour-of-day, day-of-week\n   282→   - Session indicator: Asia (00-08 UTC), Europe (08-16 UTC), US (16-00 UTC)\n   283→   - Time-to-funding: minutes until next Bybit funding rate settlement (every 8h)\n   284→\n   285→4. **Technical features** (`features/technical.py`):\n   286→   - Using pandas-ta: RSI(14), MACD(12,26,9), Bollinger(20,2), ATR(14), VWAP\n   287→   - Volume: OBV, volume-weighted momentum, volume profile\n   288→   - Returns: 1m, 5m, 15m, 30m log returns and volatility\n   289→\n   290→5. **Feature pipeline** (`features/pipeline.py`):\n   291→   - Combines all feature sets into single DataFrame\n   292→   - Handles NaN filling (forward-fill for price, zero for counts)\n   293→   - Feature normalization (rolling z-score, not global — prevents look-ahead)\n   294→   - Outputs: feature matrix aligned to 5-min prediction intervals\n   295→\n   296→### Verification\n   297→- [ ] Lead-lag correlation shows NQ leading BTC during US session (known relationship)\n   298→- [ ] Whale flow features are non-zero during known large BTC movements\n   299→- [ ] Feature pipeline produces consistent output shape\n   300→- [ ] No NaN/Inf values in output\n   301→- [ ] Rolling z-score uses only past data (no future leakage)\n   302→\n   303→---\n   304→\n   305→## Phase 6: Regime Detection\n   306→\n   307→### What to implement\n   308→1. **HMM regime detector** (`regime/detector.py`):\n   309→   - Input features: log returns, realized volatility (12-period rolling std), volume change rate\n   310→   - Fit `GaussianHMM(n_components=3, covariance_type='full', n_iter=1000)` for 3 regimes\n   311→   - Label regimes post-hoc by characteristics:\n   312→     - Trending: high absolute returns, moderate volatility\n   313→     - Mean-reverting: low returns, low volatility\n   314→     - Volatile/chaotic: high volatility, mixed returns\n   315→   - Model selection: fit n=2,3,4,5 and select by BIC\n   316→   - Pseudo-incremental update: refit every 4 hours on sliding 7-day window with `init_params=\"\"`\n   317→\n   318→2. **Regime labels** (`regime/labels.py`):\n   319→   - Map HMM state indices to semantic labels (states are arbitrary numbers)\n   320→   - Sort by volatility: lowest vol state = mean-reverting, highest = volatile\n   321→   - Provide regime probability distribution (not just hard label)\n   322→   - Regime transition probability: extract from `model.transmat_` for \"regime about to change\" signal\n   323→\n   324→### Verification\n   325→- [ ] 3 distinct regimes visible when plotted against price history\n   326→- [ ] Regime labels are stable (same market conditions → same regime across refits)\n   327→- [ ] Regime transitions align with known market events (e.g., CPI releases, ETF approvals)\n   328→- [ ] Regime probabilities sum to 1.0\n   329→\n   330→---\n   331→\n   332→## Phase 7: Models — Direction & Magnitude\n   333→\n   334→### What to implement\n   335→1. **XGBoost direction classifier** (`models/xgb_direction.py`):\n   336→   - Target: 3-class classification (up > +0.1%, down < -0.1%, flat)\n   337→   - One model per regime (3 regimes × 1 XGBoost = 3 models)\n   338→   - Features: full feature pipeline output\n   339→   - Training: sliding window walk-forward, retrain every 24h on 14-day window\n   340→   - Incremental update: `model.fit(X_new, y_new, xgb_model=model.get_booster())`\n   341→   - Feature importance tracking: log top 20 features per regime per retrain\n   342→\n   343→2. **GRU magnitude predictor** (`models/gru_magnitude.py`):\n   344→   - Target: predicted 5-min return magnitude (regression)\n   345→   - One model per regime (3 regimes × 1 GRU = 3 models)\n   346→   - Architecture: `GRU(input_size=N, hidden_size=64, num_layers=2, batch_first=True)` → `Linear(64, 1)`\n   347→   - Sequence length: 24 steps (2 hours of 5-min candles) — tune with Optuna\n   348→   - Training: sliding window, retrain every 24h, gradient clipping at 1.0\n   349→   - Never shuffle DataLoader\n   350→\n   351→3. **Regime-routed ensemble** (`models/ensemble.py`):\n   352→   - Input: current regime (from Phase 6), feature matrix\n   353→   - Route to regime-specific XGBoost + GRU pair\n   354→   - XGBoost outputs: direction (up/down/flat) + confidence (probability)\n   355→   - GRU outputs: predicted return magnitude\n   356→   - Combined signal: `direction × magnitude × confidence`\n   357→   - Confidence threshold: only emit signal when XGBoost confidence > 0.6\n   358→   - Disagreement handling: if XGBoost says up but GRU predicts negative magnitude → no signal\n   359→\n   360→### Verification\n   361→- [ ] Each regime-specific model trained on filtered data (only samples from that regime)\n   362→- [ ] Walk-forward validation shows >52% directional accuracy (above random baseline)\n   363→- [ ] Feature importance differs meaningfully across regimes\n   364→- [ ] Ensemble disagreement rate is tracked and logged\n   365→- [ ] No look-ahead bias: verify test predictions only use training data available before test timestamp\n   366→\n   367→---\n   368→\n   369→## Phase 8: Hyperparameter Tuning\n   370→\n   371→### What to implement\n   372→1. **Optuna integration** (`models/tuning.py`):\n   373→   - XGBoost search space:\n   374→     ```python\n   375→     max_depth: suggest_int(3, 12)\n   376→     learning_rate: suggest_float(0.01, 0.3, log=True)\n   377→     min_child_weight: suggest_int(1, 250)\n   378→     subsample: suggest_float(0.5, 1.0)\n   379→     colsample_bytree: suggest_float(0.5, 1.0)\n   380→     reg_lambda: suggest_float(0.001, 25.0, log=True)\n   381→     reg_alpha: suggest_float(0.001, 25.0, log=True)\n   382→     ```\n   383→   - GRU search space:\n   384→     ```python\n   385→     hidden_size: suggest_int(32, 256)\n   386→     num_layers: suggest_int(1, 3)\n   387→     lr: suggest_float(1e-5, 1e-2, log=True)\n   388→     dropout: suggest_float(0.1, 0.5)\n   389→     seq_len: suggest_int(12, 60)\n   390→     ```\n   391→   - HMM: tune `n_components` (2-5) by BIC\n   392→   - Use `MedianPruner(n_startup_trials=5, n_warmup_steps=10)` for both\n   393→   - Use `XGBoostPruningCallback` for XGBoost specifically\n   394→   - Objective: maximize walk-forward Sharpe ratio (not just accuracy)\n   395→\n   396→2. **Feature selection via tsfresh** (offline, one-time):\n   397→   - Run `extract_features` with `EfficientFCParameters` on historical data\n   398→   - Identify top statistical features (autocorrelation lags, entropy, etc.)\n   399→   - Implement top 10-15 discovered features manually in the live feature pipeline\n   400→\n   401→### Verification\n   402→- [ ] Optuna study completes 50+ trials per model\n   403→- [ ] Best hyperparameters improve Sharpe over defaults\n   404→- [ ] Pruning correctly stops poor trials early\n   405→- [ ] tsfresh features that made the cut are documented\n   406→\n   407→---\n   408→\n   409→## Phase 9: Backtesting Framework\n   410→\n   411→### What to implement\n   412→1. **Walk-forward engine** (`backtest/walk_forward.py`):\n   413→   - Custom implementation (not just sklearn TimeSeriesSplit):\n   414→     ```python\n   415→     walk_forward_validate(X, y, model, train_size=4032, test_size=288, step_size=288, gap=1)\n   416→     # 4032 = 14 days of 5-min candles, 288 = 1 day, gap=1 to prevent leakage\n   417→     ```\n   418→   - Sliding window (not expanding) — crypto regimes shift too fast\n   419→   - Re-detect regime at each step\n   420→   - Retrain regime-specific models at each step\n   421→\n   422→2. **Execution simulator** (`backtest/simulator.py`):\n   423→   - Slippage model: 0.01-0.05% per trade (configurable)\n   424→   - Transaction fees: 0.04% maker / 0.06% taker (Binance futures)\n   425→   - Latency simulation: 50-200ms delay between signal and execution\n   426→   - Position sizing: Kelly criterion or fixed fractional\n   427→   - No trading during regime transitions (confidence < threshold)\n   428→\n   429→3. **Metrics** (`backtest/metrics.py`):\n   430→   - Directional accuracy (per regime)\n   431→   - Sharpe ratio (annualized)\n   432→   - Max drawdown\n   433→   - Profit factor\n   434→   - Win rate, average win/loss ratio\n   435→   - Calmar ratio\n   436→   - Trade count per day\n   437→   - Regime accuracy (predicted vs actual)\n   438→\n   439→### Verification\n   440→- [ ] Backtest on 30+ days of historical data\n   441→- [ ] Results include transaction costs (no \"zero-cost\" delusion)\n   442→- [ ] Sharpe > 0 after costs (basic sanity)\n   443→- [ ] Compare against baselines: buy-and-hold, momentum, random\n   444→- [ ] Metrics breakdown per regime shows which regimes are profitable\n   445→\n   446→---\n   447→\n   448→## Phase 10: API & Live Prediction\n   449→\n   450→### What to implement\n   451→1. **FastAPI server** (`api/server.py`):\n   452→   - `GET /predict` — returns current prediction (direction, magnitude, confidence, regime)\n   453→   - `GET /health` — checks all data streams are alive, models are loaded, last prediction timestamp\n   454→   - `GET /metrics` — live accuracy tracking, rolling Sharpe\n   455→   - `GET /regime` — current regime + transition probabilities\n   456→   - All responses include timestamps and staleness warnings\n   457→\n   458→2. **Live prediction loop** (`scripts/live.py`):\n   459→   - Async event loop running all collectors\n   460→   - Feature pipeline triggers on each new 5-min candle close\n   461→   - Regime detection updates\n   462→   - Model inference → prediction\n   463→   - Store prediction + actual outcome for live accuracy tracking\n   464→   - Auto-retrain models every 24h on latest data\n   465→\n   466→### Verification\n   467→- [ ] API responds in < 100ms\n   468→- [ ] Health endpoint actually checks dependencies (not just returns \"ok\")\n   469→- [ ] Predictions emit within 1 second of candle close\n   470→- [ ] Live accuracy tracking matches backtest expectations (within reason)\n   471→- [ ] Graceful degradation: if one data source fails, system still produces predictions (with lower confidence)\n   472→\n   473→---\n   474→\n   475→## Phase 11: Historical Backfill & Full Validation\n   476→\n   477→### What to implement\n   478→1. **Historical data collection** (`scripts/collect_history.py`):\n   479→   - Binance REST: fetch 30-60 days of 1-min OHLCV via `exchange.fetch_ohlcv()`\n   480→   - Bybit REST: backfill OI history (`fetch_open_interest_history`) and funding rate history\n   481→   - yfinance: backfill NQ, Gold, DXY 5-min data (limited to 60 days)\n   482→   - Note: order book and trade-level data cannot be backfilled — microstructure features start from collection date\n   483→\n   484→2. **Full system validation**:\n   485→   - Run complete pipeline: ingest → features → regime → models → backtest\n   486→   - Compare regime detection against known market events\n   487→   - Validate that each edge contributes independently (ablation study):\n   488→     - Model with all features vs model without microstructure\n   489→     - Model with all features vs model without on-chain\n   490→     - Model with all features vs model without cross-market\n   491→     - Model with all features vs model without regime routing\n   492→\n   493→### Verification\n   494→- [ ] Each edge shows positive marginal contribution in ablation study\n   495→- [ ] Full system Sharpe > any single-edge system\n   496→- [ ] No edge has negative contribution (remove if so)\n   497→- [ ] System handles missing data gracefully (e.g., no on-chain data for first 30 days)\n   498→\n   499→---\n   500→\n   501→## Execution Order & Dependencies\n   502→\n   503→```\n   504→Phase 1 (Foundation)\n   505→  ↓\n   506→Phase 2 (Exchange Ingestion) ──────┐\n   507→  ↓                                 │\n   508→Phase 3 (On-Chain + Cross-Market) ─┤\n   509→  ↓                                 │\n   510→Phase 4 (Microstructure Features) ──┤── can partially parallelize\n   511→  ↓                                 │\n   512→Phase 5 (On-Chain + Cross Features)┘\n   513→  ↓\n   514→Phase 6 (Regime Detection)\n   515→  ↓\n   516→Phase 7 (Models)\n   517→  ↓\n   518→Phase 8 (Tuning)\n   519→  ↓\n   520→Phase 9 (Backtesting)\n   521→  ↓\n   522→Phase 10 (API + Live)\n   523→  ↓\n   524→Phase 11 (Validation + Ablation)\n   525→```\n   526→\n   527→Phases 2-5 can overlap: start collecting data in Phase 2-3 while building features in Phase 4-5. Models (Phase 7) need data from all feature phases.\n   528→\n   529→---\n   530→\n   531→## Key Design Decisions\n   532→\n   533→1. **Sliding window, not expanding** — crypto non-stationarity means old data hurts more than helps\n   534→2. **Per-regime models** — a trending market model is useless in a ranging market\n   535→3. **Confidence gating** — no signal is better than a low-confidence signal\n   536→4. **Magnitude + direction separation** — XGBoost excels at classification, GRU at regression\n   537→5. **15-min delay on cross-market is acceptable** — the lead-lag relationship operates on minutes-to-hours, not seconds\n   538→6. **No exchange flow data** — no free API exists; we approximate via address monitoring\n   539→7. **SQLite for dev** — zero setup, switch to TimescaleDB when moving to production\n   540→8. **Feature normalization via rolling z-score** — prevents global normalization look-ahead bias\n   541→"}]},"uuid":"5a6354c3-9a5b-444f-bbc4-685569575a44","timestamp":"2026-03-23T13:50:19.906Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"3a43ad68-a21b-4172-b054-1ace26fbde0e","userType":"external","entrypoint":"claude-vscode","cwd":"/Users/edgarpocaterra/ep2-crypto","sessionId":"f48c9af0-2e30-4c92-9024-4c84a03f39db","version":"2.1.81","gitBranch":"main","slug":"spicy-gathering-plum"}

dataclass, field\n    24→from enum import Enum\n    25→from typing import TYPE_CHECKING\n    26→\n    27→import numpy as np\n    28→import structlog\n    29→\n    30→from ep2_crypto.risk.drawdown_gate import DrawdownGate, DrawdownGateState\n    31→from ep2_crypto.risk.kill_switches import (\n    32→    KillSwitchManager,\n    33→    KillSwitchStatus,\n    34→    SwitchName,\n    35→)\n    36→from ep2_crypto.risk.position_sizer import PositionSizer, SizingResult\n    37→from ep2_crypto.risk.position_tracker import PositionSide, PositionState, PositionTracker\n    38→from ep2_crypto.risk.volatility_guard import VolatilityGuard, VolatilityGuardState\n    39→\n    40→if TYPE_CHECKING:\n    41→    from numpy.typing import NDArray\n    42→\n    43→logger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n    44→\n    45→\n    46→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    47→# Data types\n    48→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    49→\n    50→class RiskActionType(Enum):\n    51→    NONE = \"none\"\n    52→    CLOSE_POSITION = \"close_position\"\n    53→    REDUCE_POSITION = \"reduce_position\"\n    54→\n    55→\n    56→@dataclass\n    57→class RiskAction:\n    58→    \"\"\"An action the risk engine requires the execution layer to take.\"\"\"\n    59→\n    60→    action: RiskActionType\n    61→    reason: str\n    62→    urgency: str = \"normal\"  # \"normal\", \"high\", \"immediate\"\n    63→\n    64→\n    65→@dataclass\n    66→class TradeDecision:\n    67→    \"\"\"Result of approve_trade(): whether to enter and at what size.\"\"\"\n    68→\n    69→    approved: bool\n    70→    quantity_btc: float = 0.0\n    71→    notional_usd: float = 0.0\n    72→    stop_price: float = 0.0\n    73→    position_fraction: float = 0.0\n    74→    reason: str = \"\"\n    75→    sizing_details: SizingResult | None = None\n    76→\n    77→    # Breakdown of what each gate decided (for logging/debugging)\n    78→    kill_switch_ok: bool = True\n    79→    volatility_ok: bool = True\n    80→    drawdown_multiplier: float = 1.0\n    81→    vol_guard_state: VolatilityGuardState | None = None\n    82→\n    83→\n    84→@dataclass\n    85→class RiskState:\n    86→    \"\"\"Complete snapshot of risk engine state for monitoring/health endpoints.\"\"\"\n    87→\n    88→    position: PositionState\n    89→    kill_switches: list[KillSwitchStatus]\n    90→    drawdown_gate: DrawdownGateState\n    91→    equity: float\n    92→    daily_pnl: float\n    93→    weekly_pnl: float\n    94→    consecutive_losses: int\n    95→    trades_today: int\n    96→    vol_guard: VolatilityGuardState | None = None\n    97→\n    98→\n    99→@dataclass\n   100→class SignalInput:\n   101→    \"\"\"Input signal from the prediction model to the risk engine.\"\"\"\n   102→\n   103→    direction: str  # \"long\" or \"short\"\n   104→    confidence: float  # 0.0 to 1.0\n   105→    timestamp_ms: int\n   106→    win_rate: float | None = None  # historical, for Kelly\n   107→    payoff_ratio: float | None = None  # historical, for Kelly\n   108→\n   109→\n   110→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   111→# SQLite persistence for risk events\n   112→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   113→\n   114→RISK_EVENT_TABLE = \"\"\"\n   115→CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS risk_events (\n   116→    id              INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n   117→    timestamp_ms    INTEGER NOT NULL,\n   118→    event_type      TEXT    NOT NULL,\n   119→    direction       TEXT,\n   120→    confidence      REAL,\n   121→    approved        INTEGER NOT NULL,\n   122→    quantity_btc    REAL,\n   123→    stop_price      REAL,\n   124→    reason          TEXT,\n   125→    equity          REAL,\n   126→    drawdown        REAL,\n   127→    vol_annualized  REAL\n   128→)\n   129→\"\"\"\n   130→\n   131→\n   132→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   133→# RiskManager\n   134→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   135→\n   136→class RiskManager:\n   137→    \"\"\"Orchestrates all risk components.\n   138→\n   139→    Initialization requires:\n   140→        - SQLite connection (for state persistence)\n   141→        - Initial equity (capital at start)\n   142→        - Risk configuration (thresholds, sizing params)\n   143→\n   144→    Example:\n   145→        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=risk_config)\n   146→\n   147→        # Before each trade:\n   148→        decision = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, idx)\n   149→        if decision.approved:\n   150→            execute_trade(decision)\n   151→\n   152→        # On every bar:\n   153→        actions = rm.on_bar(bar_close, bar_high, bar_low, bar_ts, closes, highs, lows, idx)\n   154→        for action in actions:\n   155→            handle_action(action)\n   156→    \"\"\"\n   157→\n   158→    def __init__(\n   159→        self,\n   160→        conn: sqlite3.Connection,\n   161→        initial_equity: float,\n   162→        config: RiskConfig | None = None,\n   163→    ) -> None:\n   164→        if initial_equity <= 0:\n   165→            raise ValueError(f\"initial_equity must be positive, got {initial_equity}\")\n   166→\n   167→        self._conn = conn\n   168→        self._equity = initial_equity\n   169→        self._initial_equity = initial_equity\n   170→        self._config = config or RiskConfig()\n   171→\n   172→        # Ensure event table exists\n   173→        self._conn.execute(RISK_EVENT_TABLE)\n   174→        self._conn.commit()\n   175→\n   176→        # Initialize sub-components\n   177→        self._position = PositionTracker(conn)\n   178→        self._kill_switches = KillSwitchManager(\n   179→            conn,\n   180→            thresholds={\n   181→                \"daily_loss\": self._config.daily_loss_limit,\n   182→                \"weekly_loss\": self._config.weekly_loss_limit,\n   183→                \"max_drawdown\": self._config.max_drawdown_halt,\n   184→                \"consecutive_loss\": float(self._config.consecutive_loss_limit),\n   185→                \"emergency\": 1.0,\n   186→            },\n   187→        )\n   188→        self._drawdown_gate = DrawdownGate(\n   189→            conn,\n   190→            initial_equity=initial_equity,\n   191→            halt_threshold=self._config.max_drawdown_halt,\n   192→            cooldown_bars=self._config.drawdown_cooldown_bars,\n   193→            recovery_wins_required=self._config.drawdown_recovery_wins,\n   194→        )\n   195→        self._vol_guard = VolatilityGuard(\n   196→            min_vol_annualized=self._config.min_volatility_ann,\n   197→            max_vol_annualized=self._config.max_volatility_ann,\n   198→            trading_start_hour_utc=self._config.trading_start_hour_utc,\n   199→            trading_end_hour_utc=self._config.trading_end_hour_utc,\n   200→            weekend_reduction=self._config.weekend_size_reduction,\n   201→            enforce_trading_hours=self._config.enforce_trading_hours,\n   202→        )\n   203→        self._sizer = PositionSizer(\n   204→            kelly_fraction=self._config.kelly_fraction,\n   205→            max_position_fraction=self._config.max_position_fraction,\n   206→            min_btc_quantity=self._config.min_btc_quantity,\n   207→            atr_multiplier=self._config.atr_stop_multiplier,\n   208→            atr_period=self._config.atr_period,\n   209→            max_holding_bars=self._config.max_holding_bars,\n   210→        )\n   211→\n   212→        # Tracking counters\n   213→        self._daily_pnl: float = 0.0\n   214→        self._weekly_pnl: float = 0.0\n   215→        self._consecutive_losses: int = 0\n   216→        self._trades_today: int = 0\n   217→        self._last_stop_price: float = 0.0\n   218→\n   219→        logger.info(\n   220→            \"risk_manager_initialized\",\n   221→            initial_equity=initial_equity,\n   222→            daily_loss_limit=self._config.daily_loss_limit,\n   223→            weekly_loss_limit=self._config.weekly_loss_limit,\n   224→            max_drawdown=self._config.max_drawdown_halt,\n   225→            max_trades_per_day=self._config.max_trades_per_day,\n   226→        )\n   227→\n   228→    # -- Main entry points ----------------------------------------------------\n   229→\n   230→    def approve_trade(\n   231→        self,\n   232→        signal: SignalInput,\n   233→        closes: NDArray[np.float64],\n   234→        highs: NDArray[np.float64],\n   235→        lows: NDArray[np.float64],\n   236→        current_idx: int,\n   237→    ) -> TradeDecision:\n   238→        \"\"\"Evaluate whether a trade signal should be executed.\n   239→\n   240→        Runs all risk checks in order:\n   241→            1. Position check (already have one open?)\n   242→            2. Kill switches (any triggered?)\n   243→            3. Max trades per day\n   244→            4. Volatility guard (vol in range? hours ok?)\n   245→            5. Drawdown gate (get multiplier)\n   246→            6. Position sizing (Kelly * confidence * dd_mult * caps)\n   247→            7. Exposure check (within limits?)\n   248→\n   249→        Args:\n   250→            signal: Direction, confidence, and optional Kelly inputs.\n   251→            closes: Full close price array.\n   252→            highs: Full high price array.\n   253→            lows: Full low price array.\n   254→            current_idx: Current bar index.\n   255→\n   256→        Returns:\n   257→            TradeDecision with approval status, size, and stop price.\n   258→        \"\"\"\n   259→        # Step 0: Check if position already open\n   260→        pos = self._position.get_state()\n   261→        if pos.is_open:\n   262→            return self._reject_trade(signal, \"Position already open\")\n   263→\n   264→        # Step 1: Kill switches\n   265→        if self._kill_switches.any_triggered():\n   266→            triggered = self._kill_switches.get_triggered_names()\n   267→            return self._reject_trade(\n   268→                signal,\n   269→                f\"Kill switch(es) triggered: {', '.join(triggered)}\"\n   270→            )\n   271→\n   272→        # Step 2: Max trades per day\n   273→        if self._trades_today >= self._config.max_trades_per_day:\n   274→            return self._reject_trade(\n   275→                signal,\n   276→                f\"Max trades per day reached ({self._trades_today}/\"\n   277→                f\"{self._config.max_trades_per_day})\"\n   278→            )\n   279→\n   280→        # Step 3: Volatility guard\n   281→        vol_state = self._vol_guard.check(\n   282→            closes, current_idx, signal.timestamp_ms\n   283→        )\n   284→        if not vol_state.can_trade:\n   285→            decision = self._reject_trade(\n   286→                signal,\n   287→                vol_state.rejection_reason or \"Volatility guard rejected\",\n   288→            )\n   289→            decision.vol_guard_state = vol_state\n   290→            decision.volatility_ok = False\n   291→            return decision\n   292→\n   293→        # Step 4: Drawdown gate multiplier\n   294→        dd_mult = self._drawdown_gate.get_multiplier()\n   295→        if dd_mult <= 0.0:\n   296→            return self._reject_trade(\n   297→                signal,\n   298→                f\"Drawdown gate halted trading (multiplier={dd_mult:.4f})\",\n   299→            )\n   300→\n   301→        # Step 5: Compute time multiplier (weekend + funding)\n   302→        time_mult = vol_state.weekend_multiplier * vol_state.funding_proximity_multiplier\n   303→\n   304→        # Step 6: Position sizing\n   305→        current_price = float(closes[current_idx])\n   306→        sizing = self._sizer.compute(\n   307→            signal_direction=signal.direction,\n   308→            confidence=signal.confidence,\n   309→            equity=self._equity,\n   310→            current_price=current_price,\n   311→            highs=highs,\n   312→            lows=lows,\n   313→            closes=closes,\n   314→            current_idx=current_idx,\n   315→            drawdown_multiplier=dd_mult,\n   316→            time_multiplier=time_mult,\n   317→            win_rate=signal.win_rate,\n   318→            payoff_ratio=signal.payoff_ratio,\n   319→        )\n   320→\n   321→        if sizing.rejected:\n   322→            return self._reject_trade(\n   323→                signal,\n   324→                sizing.rejection_reason or \"Position sizer rejected\",\n   325→            )\n   326→\n   327→        # All checks passed\n   328→        decision = TradeDecision(\n   329→            approved=True,\n   330→            quantity_btc=sizing.quantity_btc,\n   331→            notional_usd=sizing.notional_usd,\n   332→            stop_price=sizing.stop_price,\n   333→            position_fraction=sizing.position_fraction,\n   334→            reason=\"All risk checks passed\",\n   335→            sizing_details=sizing,\n   336→            kill_switch_ok=True,\n   337→            volatility_ok=True,\n   338→            drawdown_multiplier=dd_mult,\n   339→            vol_guard_state=vol_state,\n   340→        )\n   341→\n   342→        self._log_event(\n   343→            event_type=\"trade_approved\",\n   344→            direction=signal.direction,\n   345→            confidence=signal.confidence,\n   346→            approved=True,\n   347→            quantity_btc=sizing.quantity_btc,\n   348→            stop_price=sizing.stop_price,\n   349→            reason=\"all_checks_passed\",\n   350→            vol_ann=vol_state.rolling_vol_annualized,\n   351→        )\n   352→\n   353→        logger.info(\n   354→            \"trade_approved\",\n   355→            direction=signal.direction,\n   356→            confidence=round(signal.confidence, 4),\n   357→            quantity_btc=round(sizing.quantity_btc, 6),\n   358→            notional_usd=round(sizing.notional_usd, 2),\n   359→            stop_price=round(sizing.stop_price, 2),\n   360→            dd_multiplier=round(dd_mult, 4),\n   361→            vol_ann=round(vol_state.rolling_vol_annualized, 4),\n   362→        )\n   363→\n   364→        return decision\n   365→\n   366→    def on_trade_opened(\n   367→        self,\n   368→        side: str,\n   369→        quantity: float,\n   370→        entry_price: float,\n   371→        entry_time_ms: int,\n   372→        stop_price: float,\n   373→    ) -> None:\n   374→        \"\"\"Notify risk engine that a trade was executed.\n   375→\n   376→        Called by the execution layer AFTER the fill is confirmed.\n   377→        \"\"\"\n   378→        self._position.open_position(side, quantity, entry_price, entry_time_ms)\n   379→        self._last_stop_price = stop_price\n   380→        self._trades_today += 1\n   381→\n   382→    def on_trade_closed(\n   383→        self,\n   384→        exit_price: float,\n   385→        exit_time_ms: int,\n   386→    ) -> float:\n   387→        \"\"\"Notify risk engine that a position was closed. Returns realized PnL.\"\"\"\n   388→        pnl = self._position.close_position(exit_price, exit_time_ms)\n   389→\n   390→        # Update tracking\n   391→        self._daily_pnl += pnl\n   392→        self._weekly_pnl += pnl\n   393→        self._equity += pnl\n   394→\n   395→        # Update consecutive losses\n   396→        if pnl < 0:\n   397→            self._consecutive_losses += 1\n   398→        else:\n   399→            self._consecutive_losses = 0\n   400→\n   401→        # Notify drawdown gate\n   402→        self._drawdown_gate.on_trade_result(profitable=(pnl > 0))\n   403→\n   404→        # Check kill switches after the trade\n   405→        self._check_all_kill_switches()\n   406→\n   407→        logger.info(\n   408→            \"trade_closed_risk_update\",\n   409→            pnl=round(pnl, 2),\n   410→            equity=round(self._equity, 2),\n   411→            daily_pnl=round(self._daily_pnl, 2),\n   412→            consecutive_losses=self._consecutive_losses,\n   413→        )\n   414→\n   415→        return pnl\n   416→\n   417→    def on_bar(\n   418→        self,\n   419→        bar_close: float,\n   420→        bar_high: float,\n   421→        bar_low: float,\n   422→        bar_timestamp_ms: int,\n   423→        closes: NDArray[np.float64],\n   424→        highs: NDArray[np.float64],\n   425→        lows: NDArray[np.float64],\n   426→        current_idx: int,\n   427→    ) -> list[RiskAction]:\n   428→        \"\"\"Process a new bar: update state, check stops, may force exits.\n   429→\n   430→        Called on every 5-min bar by the backtest engine or live loop.\n   431→\n   432→        Returns:\n   433→            List of actions for the execution layer (empty if no action needed).\n   434→        \"\"\"\n   435→        actions: list[RiskAction] = []\n   436→\n   437→        # 1. Mark position to market\n   438→        pos = self._position.mark_to_market(bar_close, bar_timestamp_ms)\n   439→\n   440→        # 2. Update equity with unrealized PnL\n   441→        unrealized = pos.unrealized_pnl if pos.is_open else 0.0\n   442→        effective_equity = self._equity + unrealized\n   443→\n   444→        # 3. Update drawdown gate\n   445→        self._drawdown_gate.update(effective_equity)\n   446→\n   447→        # 4. Check kill switches\n   448→        self._check_all_kill_switches()\n   449→        if self._kill_switches.any_triggered() and pos.is_open:\n   450→            triggered = self._kill_switches.get_triggered_names()\n   451→            actions.append(RiskAction(\n   452→                action=RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION,\n   453→                reason=f\"Kill switch triggered: {', '.join(triggered)}\",\n   454→                urgency=\"immediate\",\n   455→            ))\n   456→            return actions\n   457→\n   458→        if not pos.is_open:\n   459→            return actions\n   460→\n   461→        # 5. Check max holding period\n   462→        if pos.bars_held >= self._sizer.max_holding_bars:\n   463→            actions.append(RiskAction(\n   464→                action=RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION,\n   465→                reason=(\n   466→                    f\"Max holding period exceeded: {pos.bars_held} bars \"\n   467→                    f\">= {self._sizer.max_holding_bars}\"\n   468→                ),\n   469→                urgency=\"high\",\n   470→            ))\n   471→            return actions\n   472→\n   473→        # 6. Check stop loss\n   474→        if self._last_stop_price > 0:\n   475→            stopped = False\n   476→            if pos.side == PositionSide.LONG and bar_low <= self._last_stop_price:\n   477→                stopped = True\n   478→            elif pos.side == PositionSide.SHORT and bar_high >= self._last_stop_price:\n   479→                stopped = True\n   480→\n   481→            if stopped:\n   482→                actions.append(RiskAction(\n   483→                    action=RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION,\n   484→                    reason=(\n   485→                        f\"Stop loss hit: stop={self._last_stop_price:.2f}, \"\n   486→                        f\"bar_low={bar_low:.2f}, bar_high={bar_high:.2f}\"\n   487→                    ),\n   488→                    urgency=\"immediate\",\n   489→                ))\n   490→                return actions\n   491→\n   492→        return actions\n   493→\n   494→    # -- State access ---------------------------------------------------------\n   495→\n   496→    def get_risk_state(self) -> RiskState:\n   497→        \"\"\"Return complete risk engine state for monitoring.\"\"\"\n   498→        pos = self._position.get_state()\n   499→        unrealized = pos.unrealized_pnl if pos.is_open else 0.0\n   500→\n   501→        return RiskState(\n   502→            position=pos,\n   503→            kill_switches=self._kill_switches.get_all_status(),\n   504→            drawdown_gate=self._drawdown_gate.get_state(),\n   505→            equity=self._equity + unrealized,\n   506→            daily_pnl=self._daily_pnl + unrealized,\n   507→            weekly_pnl=self._weekly_pnl + unrealized,\n   508→            consecutive_losses=self._consecutive_losses,\n   509→            trades_today=self._trades_today,\n   510→        )\n   511→\n   512→    def get_equity(self) -> float:\n   513→        \"\"\"Return current equity (realized only, no unrealized).\"\"\"\n   514→        return self._equity\n   515→\n   516→    def get_position(self) -> PositionState:\n   517→        \"\"\"Return current position state.\"\"\"\n   518→        return self._position.get_state()\n   519→\n   520→    # -- Day/week boundary management -----------------------------------------\n   521→\n   522→    def reset_daily_counters(self) -> None:\n   523→        \"\"\"Call at day boundary (00:00 UTC) to reset daily limits.\"\"\"\n   524→        logger.info(\n   525→            \"daily_counters_reset\",\n   526→            previous_daily_pnl=round(self._daily_pnl, 2),\n   527→            trades_today=self._trades_today,\n   528→        )\n   529→        self._daily_pnl = 0.0\n   530→        self._trades_today = 0\n   531→        self._position.reset_daily_pnl()\n   532→\n   533→    def reset_weekly_counters(self) -> None:\n   534→        \"\"\"Call at week boundary (Monday 00:00 UTC) to reset weekly limits.\"\"\"\n   535→        logger.info(\n   536→            \"weekly_counters_reset\",\n   537→            previous_weekly_pnl=round(self._weekly_pnl, 2),\n   538→        )\n   539→        self._weekly_pnl = 0.0\n   540→\n   541→    # -- Kill switch delegation -----------------------------------------------\n   542→\n   543→    def reset_kill_switch(self, switch_name: SwitchName, reason: str) -> None:\n   544→        \"\"\"Reset a specific kill switch. Requires reason string.\"\"\"\n   545→        self._kill_switches.reset(switch_name, reason)\n   546→\n   547→    def trigger_emergency(self, reason: str) -> None:\n   548→        \"\"\"Trigger emergency kill switch.\"\"\"\n   549→        self._kill_switches.trigger_emergency(reason, equity=self._equity)\n   550→\n   551→    # -- Private helpers -------------------------------------------------------\n   552→\n   553→    def _reject_trade(self, signal: SignalInput, reason: str) -> TradeDecision:\n   554→        \"\"\"Create a rejected trade decision and log it.\"\"\"\n   555→        self._log_event(\n   556→            event_type=\"trade_rejected\",\n   557→            direction=signal.direction,\n   558→            confidence=signal.confidence,\n   559→            approved=False,\n   560→            quantity_btc=0.0,\n   561→            stop_price=0.0,\n   562→            reason=reason,\n   563→        )\n   564→        logger.info(\n   565→            \"trade_rejected\",\n   566→            direction=signal.direction,\n   567→            confidence=round(signal.confidence, 4),\n   568→            reason=reason,\n   569→        )\n   570→        return TradeDecision(approved=False, reason=reason)\n   571→\n   572→    def _check_all_kill_switches(self) -> None:\n   573→        \"\"\"Run all kill switch checks against current state.\"\"\"\n   574→        self._kill_switches.check_daily_loss(\n   575→            daily_pnl_fraction=self._daily_pnl / self._initial_equity,\n   576→            equity=self._equity,\n   577→        )\n   578→        self._kill_switches.check_weekly_loss(\n   579→            weekly_pnl_fraction=self._weekly_pnl / self._initial_equity,\n   580→            equity=self._equity,\n   581→        )\n   582→        self._kill_switches.check_max_drawdown(\n   583→            drawdown_fraction=self._drawdown_gate.get_drawdown(),\n   584→            equity=self._equity,\n   585→        )\n   586→        self._kill_switches.check_consecutive_losses(\n   587→            consecutive_losses=self._consecutive_losses,\n   588→            equity=self._equity,\n   589→        )\n   590→\n   591→    def _log_event(\n   592→        self,\n   593→        event_type: str,\n   594→        direction: str | None = None,\n   595→        confidence: float | None = None,\n   596→        approved: bool = False,\n   597→        quantity_btc: float | None = None,\n   598→        stop_price: float | None = None,\n   599→        reason: str | None = None,\n   600→        vol_ann: float | None = None,\n   601→    ) -> None:\n   602→        \"\"\"Persist a risk event to SQLite.\"\"\"\n   603→        now_ms = int(time.time() * 1000)\n   604→        dd = self._drawdown_gate.get_drawdown()\n   605→        self._conn.execute(\n   606→            \"INSERT INTO risk_events \"\n   607→            \"(timestamp_ms, event_type, direction, confidence, approved, \"\n   608→            \"quantity_btc, stop_price, reason, equity, drawdown, vol_annualized) \"\n   609→            \"VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\",\n   610→            (\n   611→                now_ms,\n   612→                event_type,\n   613→                direction,\n   614→                confidence,\n   615→                int(approved),\n   616→                quantity_btc,\n   617→                stop_price,\n   618→                reason,\n   619→                self._equity,\n   620→                dd,\n   621→                vol_ann,\n   622→  self,\n   254→        switch_name: SwitchName,\n   255→        reason: str,\n   256→    ) -> None:\n   257→        \"\"\"Reset a triggered kill switch back to ARMED.\n   258→\n   259→        Args:\n ValueError: If the switch is not currently triggered.\n   265→        \"\"\"\n   266→        row = self._conn.execute(\n   267→            \"SELECT state FROM risk_kill_switches WHERE name = ?\",\n   268→            (switch_name,),\n   269→        ).fetchone()\n   270→        if row is None:\n   271→            raise ValueError(f\"Unknown kill switch: {switch_name}\")\n   272→        if row[0] != {"parentUuid":"6d0e240b-ff15-49b3-a918-2bfc7843f18a","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"dfb178e0-4750-4e30-89d2-a96d8e042d19","agentId":"a78bdc2b5817029ed","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01QBuA8HsL8Cqh6ukckccUmq","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→\"\"\"Drawdown-based position size gating with continuous multiplier.\n     2→\n     3→Tracks peak equity and computes a position-size multiplier that decreases\n     4→continuously as drawdown increases. Uses a smooth exponential decay rather\n     5→than hard steps, so there are no cliff edges in sizing behavior.\n     6→\n     7→The multiplier curve:\n     8→    - 0% drawdown  -> 1.0x (full size)\n     9→    - 3% drawdown  -> 0.75x\n    10→    - 5% drawdown  -> 0.50x\n    11→    - 10% drawdown -> 0.25x\n    12→    - 15% drawdown -> 0.0x  (halt)\n    13→\n    14→Between these points the function interpolates smoothly using a fitted\n    15→exponential: multiplier = max(0, 1 - (dd / halt_threshold)^alpha)\n    16→where alpha is calibrated to pass through the reference points.\n    17→\n    18→Recovery logic:\n    19→    After drawdown recovers, the multiplier does NOT snap back immediately.\n    20→    A cooldown period (minimum_cooldown_bars) must elapse at the reduced\n    21→    level before the multiplier starts increasing. As drawdown deepens, the multiplier shrinks.\n    77→\n    78→    Configuration:\n    79→        halt_threshold: drawdown fraction at which multiplier = 0 (default 0.15)\n    80→        decay_alpha: profitable trades needed for full recovery (default 5)\n    83→\n    84→    The decay_alpha of 1.8 produces a curve that approximately passes through:\n    85→        dd=0.03 -> 0.76, dd=0.05 -> 0.60, dd=0.10 -> 0.28, dd=0.15 -> 0.00\n    86→    Close to the specified step function but smooth.\n    87→    \"\"\"\n    88→\n    89→    def __init__(\n    90→        self,\n    91→        conn: effective, only increase\n   150→        # after cooldown expires and we have enough recovery wins\n   151→        if raw_mult > self._effective_multiplier:\n   152→            # Drawdown is recovering\n   153→            if self._cooldown_remaining > 0:\n   154→                self._cooldown_remaining -= 1\n   155→                # Keep the effective multiplier at the lower level during cooldown\n   156→                new_mult = self._effective_multiplier\n   157→            elif self._recovery_wins >= self._recovery_wins_required:\n   158→                # Full recovery: snap to \"drawdown_gate_recovery_complete\",\n   163→                    multiplier=round(new_mult, 4),\n   164→                    drawdown=round(dd, 4),\n   165→                )\n   166→            else:\n self._effective_multiplier + progress * (\n   170→                    raw_mult - self._effective_multiplier\n   171→                )\n   172→        elif raw_mult < self._effective_multiplier:\n   173→            # Drawdown is deepening: apply new lower multiplier immediately\n   174→            new_mult = raw_mult\n   175→            self._cooldown_remaining = self._cooldown_bars  # reset max(0.0, (self._peak_equity - self._current_equity) / self._peak_equity)\n   235→\n   236→    # -- Private helpers -------------------------------------------------------\n   237→\n   238→    def _compute_multiplier(self, drawdown: float) -> float:\n   239→        \"\"\"Compute raw multiplier from drawdown using smooth decay.\n   240→\n   241→        multiplier = max(0, 1 - (dd / halt_threshold)^alpha)\n   242→\n   243→        With alpha=1.8 and halt=0.15:\n   244→            dd=0.00 -> 1.000\n   245→            dd=0.03 -> 0.759\n   246→            dd=0.05 -> 0.592\n   247→            dd=0.10 -> 0.276\n   248→            dd=0.15 -> 0.000\n   249→        \"\"\"\n   250→        if drawdown <= 0:\n   251→            return 1.0\n   252→        if drawdown >= Here is the complete research document.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Essential Real-Time Risk Metrics\n\n### Prometheus Metric Definitions\n\nEvery metric uses the `ep2_` prefix for namespace isolation. Labels use `symbol` (default `BTCUSDT`) to support future multi-asset.\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/metrics_exporter.py\n\nfrom prometheus_client import Gauge, Counter, Histogram, Info, Summary\n\n# ── Position metrics ──\nep2_position_side = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_position_side\",\n    \"Current position direction: 1=long, -1=short, 0=flat\",\n    [\"symbol\"],\n)\nep2_position_quantity_btc = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_position_quantity_btc\",\n    \"Current position size in BTC\",\n    [\"symbol\"],\n)\nep2_position_entry_price = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_position_entry_price\",\n    \"Entry price of current position in USD\",\n    [\"symbol\"],\n)\nep2_position_notional_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_position_notional_usd\",\n    \"Dollar notional of current position\",\n    [\"symbol\"],\n)\nep2_position_unrealized_pnl_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_position_unrealized_pnl_usd\",\n    \"Unrealized PnL of current position in USD\",\n    [\"symbol\"],\n)\nep2_position_bars_held = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_position_bars_held\",\n    \"Number of 5-min bars the current position has been held\",\n    [\"symbol\"],\n)\nep2_position_holding_duration_seconds = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_position_holding_duration_seconds\",\n    \"Duration of current open position in seconds\",\n    [\"symbol\"],\n)\n\n# ──
