[\"symbol\"],\n)\nep2_liquidation_distance_pct = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_liquidation_distance_pct\",\n    \"Distance from current price to estimated liquidation price as percentage\",\n    [\"symbol\"],\n)\n\n# ── PnL metrics ──\nep2_daily_pnl_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_daily_pnl_usd\",\n    \"Today's realized + unrealized PnL in USD\",\n)\nep2_weekly_pnl_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_weekly_pnl_usd\",\n    \"Rolling 7-day PnL in USD\",\n)\nep2_equity_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_equity_usd\",\n    \"Current total equity including unrealized PnL\",\n)\nep2_peak_equity_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_peak_equity_usd\",\n    \"All-time peak equity for drawdown calculation\",\n)\n\n# ── Drawdown ──\nep2_drawdown_from_peak_pct = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_drawdown_from_peak_pct\",\n    \"Current drawdown from equity peak as percentage (positive = losing)\",\n)\nep2_drawdown_gate_multiplier = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_drawdown_gate_multiplier\",\n    \"Position size multiplier from drawdown gate (0.0 to 1.0)\",\n)\n\n# ── Margin ──\nep2_margin_utilization_pct = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_margin_utilization_pct\",\n    \"Percentage of available margin currently used\",\n    [\"symbol\"],\n)\n\n# ── Kill switch status ──\nep2_kill_switch_triggered = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_kill_switch_triggered\",\n    \"1 if this kill switch is triggered, 0 if armed\",\n [\"switch_name\"],\n)\nep2_kill_switch_threshold = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_kill_switch_threshold\",\n    \"Threshold at which this switch triggers\",\n    [\"switch_name\"],\n)\n\n# ── Trade counters ──\nep2_trades_today_total = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_trades_today_total\",\n    \"Number of trades executed today\",\n)\nep2_trades_total = Counter(\n    \"ep2_trades_total\",\n    \"Cumulative trade count since startup\",\n    [\"side\", \"result\"],  # result: \"win\" or \"loss\"\n)\nep2_consecutive_losses = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_consecutive_losses\",\n    \"Current consecutive losing trade streak\",\n)\n```\n\n### Python Exporter Code\n\nThis class reads from your existing `RiskManager.get_risk_state()` and pushes to Prometheus on every bar:\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/metrics_exporter.py (continued)\n\nimport structlog\n\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.kill_switches import SwitchState\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.position_tracker import PositionSide\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.risk_manager import RiskManager, RiskState\n\nlogger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n\nSIDE_MAP = {\n    PositionSide.LONG: 1.0,\n    PositionSide.SHORT: -1.0,\n    PositionSide.FLAT: 0.0,\n}\n\n\nclass PrometheusRiskExporter:\n    \"\"\"Reads RiskState from RiskManager and updates Prometheus gauges.\n\n    Call `export()` on every 5-min bar. The exporter is stateless --\n    it reads whatever the RiskManager currently reports and sets gauges.\n\n    Integration:\n        exporter = PrometheusRiskExporter(risk_manager, symbol=\"BTCUSDT\")\n        # In the bar loop:\n        exporter.export(current_price, stop_price, liquidation_price)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        risk_manager: RiskManager,\n        symbol: str = \"BTCUSDT\",\n    ) -> None:\n        self._rm = risk_manager\n        self._symbol = symbol\n\n    def export(\n        self,\n        current_price: float,\n        stop_price: float = 0.0,\n        liquidation_price: float = 0.0,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Update all Prometheus gauges from current risk state.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            state: RiskState = self._rm.get_risk_state()\n            self._export_position(state, current_price, stop_price, liquidation_price)\n            self._export_pnl(state)\n            self._export_drawdown(state)\n            self._export_kill_switches(state)\n            self._export_counters(state)\n        except Exception:\n            logger.exception(\"prometheus_export_failed\")\n\n    def _export_position(\n        self,\n        state: RiskState,\n        current_price: float,\n        stop_price: float,\n        liquidation_price: float,\n    ) -> None:\n        pos = state.position\n        ep2_position_side.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(\n            SIDE_MAP.get(pos.side, 0.0)\n        )\n        ep2_position_quantity_btc.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(pos.quantity)\n        ep2_position_entry_price.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(pos.entry_price)\n        ep2_position_notional_usd.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(pos.notional_usd)\n        ep2_position_unrealized_pnl_usd.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(\n            pos.unrealized_pnl\n        )\n        ep2_position_bars_held.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(pos.bars_held)\n\n        if pos.is_open and pos.entry_time_ms > 0:\n            import time\n            duration_s = (int(time.time() * 1000) - pos.entry_time_ms) / 1000.0\n            ep2_position_holding_duration_seconds.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(\n                duration_s\n            )\n        else:\n            ep2_position_holding_duration_seconds.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(0)\n\n        # Stop distance\n        if stop_price > 0 and current_price > 0:\n            stop_dist = abs(current_price - stop_price) / current_price * 100\n            ep2_stop_distance_pct.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(stop_dist)\n\n        # Liquidation distance\n        if liquidation_price > 0 and current_price > 0:\n            liq_dist = abs(current_price - liquidation_price) / current_price * 100\n            ep2_liquidation_distance_pct.labels(symbol=self._symbol).set(liq_dist)\n\n    def _export_pnl(self, state: RiskState) -> None:\n        ep2_daily_pnl_usd.set(state.daily_pnl)\n        ep2_weekly_pnl_usd.set(state.weekly_pnl)\n        ep2_equity_usd.set(state.equity)\n        ep2_peak_equity_usd.set(state.drawdown_gate.peak_equity)\n\n    def _export_drawdown(self, state: RiskState) -> None:\n        dd_pct = state.drawdown_gate.current_drawdown * 100\n        ep2_drawdown_from_peak_pct.set(dd_pct)\n        ep2_drawdown_gate_multiplier.set(state.drawdown_gate.current_multiplier)\n\n    def _export_kill_switches(self, state: RiskState) -> None:\n        for ks in state.kill_switches:\n            triggered = 1.0 if ks.state == SwitchState.TRIGGERED else 0.0\n            ep2_kill_switch_triggered.labels(switch_name=ks.name).set(triggered)\n            ep2_kill_switch_current_value.labels(switch_name=ks.name).set(\n                ks.current_value\n            )\n            ep2_kill_switch_threshold.labels(switch_name=ks.name).set(ks.threshold)\n\n    def _export_counters(self, state: RiskState) -> None:\n        ep2_trades_today_total.set(state.trades_today)\n        ep2_consecutive_losses.set(state.consecutive_losses)\n```\n\n### Grafana Panel Configuration (Row 1: Position Status)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Current Position\",\n  \"type\": \"stat\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_position_side{symbol=\\\"BTCUSDT\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Direction\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_position_quantity_btc{symbol=\\\"BTCUSDT\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Size BTC\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_position_entry_price{symbol=\\\"BTCUSDT\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Entry\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_position_unrealized_pnl_usd{symbol=\\\"BTCUSDT\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Unrealized PnL\" }\n        ]\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Distance to Stop / Liquidation\",\n  \"type\": \"gauge\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_stop_distance_pct{symbol=\\\"BTCUSDT\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Stop Distance %\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_liquidation_distance_pct{symbol=\\\"BTCUSDT\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Liq Distance %\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"min\": 0, \"max\": 10,\n      \"thresholds\": {\n        \"steps\": [\n          { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"red\" },\n          { \"value\": 1.5, \"color\": \"yellow\" },\n          { \"value\": 3.0, \"color\": \"green\" }\n        ]\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Rolling Performance Metrics\n\n### Prometheus Metric Definitions\n\n```python\n# ── Rolling performance (updated after each trade or on schedule) ──\nep2_rolling_sharpe = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_rolling_sharpe\",\n    \"Rolling Sharpe ratio (annualized with sqrt(105120))\",\n    [\"window\"],  # \"7d\", \"30d\"\n)\nep2_rolling_win_rate = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_rolling_win_rate\",\n    \"Win rate over rolling window\",\n    [\"window\"],\n)\nep2_rolling_max_drawdown_pct = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_rolling_max_drawdown_pct\",\n    \"Maximum drawdown within the rolling window as percentage\",\n    [\"window\"],\n)\nep2_rolling_profit_factor = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_rolling_profit_factor\",\n    \"Gross profit / gross loss over rolling window\",\n    [\"window\"],\n)\nep2_rolling_trades_per_day = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_rolling_trades_per_day\",\n    \"Average trades per day over rolling window\",\n    [\"window\"],\n)\nep2_rolling_avg_trade_pnl_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_rolling_avg_trade_pnl_usd\",\n    \"Average PnL per trade over rolling window in USD\",\n    [\"window\"],\n)\nep2_rolling_avg_trade_pnl_bps = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_rolling_avg_trade_pnl_bps\",\n    \"Average PnL per trade in basis points\",\n    [\"window\"],\n)\n```\n\n### Rolling Metrics Calculator\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/rolling_performance.py\n\nimport sqlite3\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport structlog\n\nlogger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n\nCRYPTO_ANNUALIZATION = 324.22  # sqrt(105120) for 5-min bars, 24/7\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass RollingMetrics:\n    \"\"\"Performance metrics over a rolling window.\"\"\"\n    sharpe: float\n    win_rate: float\n    max_drawdown_pct: float\n    profit_factor: float\n    trades_per_day: float\n    avg_trade_pnl_usd: float\n    avg_trade_pnl_bps: float\n    total_trades: int\n    window_label: str\n\n\nclass RollingPerformanceCalculator:\n    \"\"\"Computes rolling performance metrics from the trade log in SQLite.\n\n    Reads closed trades from the risk_events table and computes\n    windowed statistics. Call `compute()` periodically (every bar or\n    every N minutes).\n\n    The 7d and 30d windows are critical for detecting alpha decay.\n    If 7d Sharpe drops below 0.3 while 30d is above 1.0, the recent\n    regime may be unfavorable and the model may need retraining.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:\n        self._conn = conn\n\n    def compute(self, window_days: int, window_label: str) -> RollingMetrics:\n        \"\"\"Compute rolling metrics over the last N days of trades.\n\n        Args:\n            window_days: Number of calendar days to look back.\n            window_label: Label for Prometheus (e.g., \"7d\", \"30d\").\n\n        Returns:\n            RollingMetrics with all computed values.\n        \"\"\"\n        import time\n        cutoff_ms = int((time.time() - window_days * 86400) * 1000)\n\n        # Fetch PnL values for closed trades in window.\n        # This assumes a trade_log table. Alternatively, parse risk_events.\n        rows = self._conn.execute(\n            \"SELECT quantity_btc, stop_price, equity, drawdown \"\n            \"FROM risk_events \"\n            \"WHERE event_type = 'trade_closed' AND timestamp_ms >= ? \"\n            \"ORDER BY timestamp_ms ASC\",\n            (cutoff_ms,),\n        ).fetchall()\n\n        # If you have a dedicated trade_log table with pnl column, use that instead.\n        # Fallback: compute from equity curve\n        pnls = np.array([row[0] for row in rows], dtype=np.float64) if rows else np.array([])\n\n        total_trades = len(pnls)\n        if total_trades == 0:\n            return RollingMetrics(\n                sharpe=0.0, win_rate=0.0, max_drawdown_pct=0.0,\n                profit_factor=0.0, trades_per_day=0.0,\n                avg_trade_pnl_usd=0.0, avg_trade_pnl_bps=0.0,\n                total_trades=0, window_label=window_label,\n            )\n\n        wins = pnls[pnls > 0]\n        losses = pnls[pnls < 0]\n        win_rate = len(wins) / total_trades if total_trades > 0 else 0.0\n        gross_profit = float(np.sum(wins)) if len(wins) > 0 else 0.0\n        gross_loss = float(np.abs(np.sum(losses))) if len(losses) > 0 else 0.0\n        profit_factor = gross_profit / gross_loss if gross_loss > 0 else float(\"inf\")\n\n        avg_pnl = float(np.mean(pnls))\n        std_pnl = float(np.std(pnls, ddof=1)) if total_trades > 1 else 1.0\n\n        # Sharpe: annualize using bars per year (not sqrt(252))\n        bars_per_trade = 3  # approximate average bars per trade\n        trades_per_year = 105120 / bars_per_trade\n        sharpe = (avg_pnl / std_pnl) * np.sqrt(trades_per_year) if std_pnl > 0 else 0.0\n\n        trades_per_day = total_trades / window_days\n\n        # Max drawdown within the window (from cumulative PnL)\n        cum_pnl = np.cumsum(pnls)\n        running_max = np.maximum.accumulate(cum_pnl)\n        dd_curve = running_max - cum_pnl\n        max_dd = float(np.max(dd_curve)) if len(dd_curve) > 0 else 0.0\n        peak_val = float(np.max(running_max)) if len(running_max) > 0 else 1.0\n        max_dd_pct = (max_dd / peak_val * 100) if peak_val > 0 else 0.0\n\n        return RollingMetrics(\n            sharpe=float(sharpe),\n            win_rate=win_rate,\n            max_drawdown_pct=max_dd_pct,\n            profit_factor=profit_factor,\n            trades_per_day=trades_per_day,\n            avg_trade_pnl_usd=avg_pnl,\n            avg_trade_pnl_bps=avg_pnl * 10000 / 50000,  # relative to typical capital\n            total_trades=total_trades,\n            window_label=window_label,\n        )\n\n    def export_to_prometheus(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Compute and export 7d and 30d rolling metrics.\"\"\"\n        for days, label in [(7, \"7d\"), (30, \"30d\")]:\n            m = self.compute(days, label)\n            ep2_rolling_sharpe.labels(window=label).set(m.sharpe)\n            ep2_rolling_win_rate.labels(window=label).set(m.win_rate)\n            ep2_rolling_max_drawdown_pct.labels(window=label).set(m.max_drawdown_pct)\n            ep2_rolling_profit_factor.labels(window=label).set(m.profit_factor)\n            ep2_rolling_trades_per_day.labels(window=label).set(m.trades_per_day)\n            ep2_rolling_avg_trade_pnl_usd.labels(window=label).set(m.avg_trade_pnl_usd)\n            ep2_rolling_avg_trade_pnl_bps.labels(window=label).set(m.avg_trade_pnl_bps)\n```\n\n### Grafana Panel Configuration (Row 2: Rolling Performance)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Rolling Sharpe Ratio\",\n  \"type\": \"timeseries\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_rolling_sharpe{window=\\\"7d\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"7d Sharpe\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_rolling_sharpe{window=\\\"30d\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"30d Sharpe\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"custom\": { \"lineWidth\": 2, \"fillOpacity\": 10 },\n      \"thresholds\": {\n        \"mode\": \"absolute\",\n        \"steps\": [\n          { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"red\" },\n          { \"value\": 0.5, \"color\": \"yellow\" },\n          { \"value\": 1.0, \"color\": \"green\" }\n        ]\n      }\n    }\n  },\n  \"options\": {\n    \"tooltip\": { \"mode\": \"multi\" }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Rolling Stats Table\",\n  \"type\": \"table\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_rolling_win_rate\", \"legendFormat\": \"Win Rate\", \"format\": \"table\", \"instant\": true },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_rolling_profit_factor\", \"legendFormat\": \"Profit Factor\", \"format\": \"table\", \"instant\": true },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_rolling_trades_per_day\", \"legendFormat\": \"Trades/Day\", \"format\": \"table\", \"instant\": true },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_rolling_avg_trade_pnl_bps\", \"legendFormat\": \"Avg PnL (bps)\", \"format\": \"table\", \"instant\": true }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Risk State Visualization (Traffic Light System)\n\n### Prometheus Metrics\n\n```python\n# ── Overall risk state ──\nep2_risk_state = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_risk_state\",\n    \"Overall risk state: 0=green, 1=yellow, 2=red, 3=emergency\",\n)\nep2_daily_loss_budget_remaining_pct = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_daily_loss_budget_remaining_pct\",\n    \"Percentage of daily loss budget remaining (100% = no losses today)\",\n)\nep2_volatility_annualized = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_volatility_annualized\",\n    \"Current rolling annualized volatility\",\n)\nep2_volatility_state = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_volatility_state\",\n    \"Volatility regime: 0=low, 1=normal, 2=high, 3=extreme\",\n)\n```\n\n### Risk State Engine\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/risk_state_engine.py\n\nfrom enum import IntEnum\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\n\nimport structlog\n\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.risk_manager import RiskState\n\nlogger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n\n\nclass RiskLevel(IntEnum):\n    GREEN = 0       # All systems nominal\n    YELLOW = 1      # Caution: approaching limits\n    RED = 2         # Danger: at or near limits\n    EMERGENCY = 3   # System halt\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass RiskStateAssessment:\n    \"\"\"Complete risk state assessment with per-component breakdown.\"\"\"\n    overall: RiskLevel\n    drawdown_level: RiskLevel\n    daily_loss_level: RiskLevel\n    consecutive_loss_level: RiskLevel\n    kill_switch_level: RiskLevel\n    volatility_level: RiskLevel\n    reasons: list[str]\n\n\nclass RiskStateEngine:\n    \"\"\"Evaluates overall system risk level from component states.\n\n    Thresholds are calibrated for the ep2-crypto system's risk parameters:\n        - Daily loss limit: 3% (from CLAUDE.md)\n        - Max drawdown halt: 15%\n        - Consecutive loss limit: 15\n\n    Traffic light rules:\n        GREEN:      dd < 3%, daily_loss < 1%, consec_losses < 5\n        YELLOW:     dd 3-7%, daily_loss 1-2%, consec_losses 5-10\n        RED:        dd 7-12%, daily_loss 2-2.5%, consec_losses 10-15\n        EMERGENCY:  dd > 12%, daily_loss > 2.5%, any kill switch triggered\n\n    The overall state is the WORST of all components.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def assess(self, state: RiskState) -> RiskStateAssessment:\n        reasons: list[str] = []\n\n        # Check each component\n        dd_pct = state.drawdown_gate.current_drawdown * 100\n        dd_level = self._assess_drawdown(dd_pct, reasons)\n\n        daily_loss_pct = abs(min(state.daily_pnl, 0)) / max(state.equity, 1) * 100\n        daily_level = self._assess_daily_loss(daily_loss_pct, reasons)\n\n        consec_level = self._assess_consecutive(state.consecutive_losses, reasons)\n        ks_level = self._assess_kill_switches(state, reasons)\n        vol_level = RiskLevel.GREEN  # computed separately from volatility guard\n\n        overall = max(dd_level, daily_level, consec_level, ks_level, vol_level)\n\n        return RiskStateAssessment(\n            overall=overall,\n            drawdown_level=dd_level,\n            daily_loss_level=daily_level,\n            consecutive_loss_level=consec_level,\n            kill_switch_level=ks_level,\n            volatility_level=vol_level,\n            reasons=reasons,\n        )\n\n    def _assess_drawdown(self, dd_pct: float, reasons: list[str]) -> RiskLevel:\n        if dd_pct >= 12:\n            reasons.append(f\"EMERGENCY: Drawdown {dd_pct:.1f}% approaching halt\")\n            return RiskLevel.EMERGENCY\n        if dd_pct >= 7:\n            reasons.append(f\"RED: Drawdown {dd_pct:.1f}%\")\n            return RiskLevel.RED\n        if dd_pct >= 3:\n            reasons.append(f\"YELLOW: Drawdown {dd_pct:.1f}%\")\n            return RiskLevel.YELLOW\n        return RiskLevel.GREEN\n\n    def _assess_daily_loss(self, loss_pct: float, reasons: list[str]) -> RiskLevel:\n        if loss_pct >= 2.5:\n            reasons.append(f\"EMERGENCY: Daily loss {loss_pct:.1f}%\")\n            return RiskLevel.EMERGENCY\n        if loss_pct >= 2.0:\n            reasons.append(f\"RED: Daily loss {loss_pct:.1f}%\")\n            return RiskLevel.RED\n        if loss_pct >= 1.0:\n            reasons.append(f\"YELLOW: Daily loss {loss_pct:.1f}%\")\n            return RiskLevel.YELLOW\n        return RiskLevel.GREEN\n\n    def _assess_consecutive(self, count: int, reasons: list[str]) -> RiskLevel:\n        if count >= 15:\n            reasons.append(f\"EMERGENCY: {count} consecutive losses\")\n            return RiskLevel.EMERGENCY\n        if count >= 10:\n            reasons.append(f\"RED: {count} consecutive losses\")\n            return RiskLevel.RED\n        if count >= 5:\n            reasons.append(f\"YELLOW: {count} consecutive losses\")\n            return RiskLevel.YELLOW\n        return RiskLevel.GREEN\n\n    def _assess_kill_switches(\n        self, state: RiskState, reasons: list[str]\n    ) -> RiskLevel:\n        from ep2_crypto.risk.kill_switches import SwitchState\n        triggered = [\n            ks.name for ks in state.kill_switches\n            if ks.state == SwitchState.TRIGGERED\n        ]\n        if triggered:\n            reasons.append(f\"EMERGENCY: Kill switches active: {', '.join(triggered)}\")\n            return RiskLevel.EMERGENCY\n        return RiskLevel.GREEN\n\n    def export_to_prometheus(self, state: RiskState) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Export the risk state assessment to Prometheus.\"\"\"\n        assessment = self.assess(state)\n        ep2_risk_state.set(assessment.overall.value)\n\n        # Daily loss budget\n        initial_equity = state.drawdown_gate.peak_equity\n        daily_limit_usd = initial_equity * 0.03  # 3% from config\n        used = abs(min(state.daily_pnl, 0))\n        remaining_pct = max(0, (1.0 - used / daily_limit_usd) * 100) if daily_limit_usd > 0 else 0\n        ep2_daily_loss_budget_remaining_pct.set(remaining_pct)\n```\n\n### Grafana Panel Configuration (Row 3: Traffic Light)\n\n**Traffic Light Stat Panel:**\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"System Risk State\",\n  \"type\": \"stat\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_risk_state\", \"legendFormat\": \"Risk Level\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"mappings\": [\n        { \"type\": \"value\", \"options\": { \"0\": { \"text\": \"GREEN\", \"color\": \"green\" } } },\n        { \"type\": \"value\", \"options\": { \"1\": { \"text\": \"YELLOW\", \"color\": \"yellow\" } } },\n        { \"type\": \"value\", \"options\": { \"2\": { \"text\": \"RED\", \"color\": \"red\" } } },\n        { \"type\": \"value\", \"options\": { \"3\": { \"text\": \"EMERGENCY\", \"color\": \"dark-red\" } } }\n      ],\n      \"thresholds\": {\n        \"steps\": [\n          { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"green\" },\n          { \"value\": 1, \"color\": \"yellow\" },\n          { \"value\": 2, \"color\": \"red\" },\n          { \"value\": 3, \"color\": \"dark-red\" }\n        ]\n      }\n    }\n  },\n  \"options\": { \"graphMode\": \"none\", \"textMode\": \"value_and_name\" }\n}\n```\n\n**Drawdown Gauge Panel:**\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Drawdown Gauge\",\n  \"type\": \"gauge\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_drawdown_from_peak_pct\", \"legendFormat\": \"Drawdown %\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"min\": 0, \"max\": 20,\n      \"thresholds\": {\n        \"steps\": [\n          { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"green\" },\n          { \"value\": 3, \"color\": \"yellow\" },\n          { \"value\": 7, \"color\": \"orange\" },\n          { \"value\": 12, \"color\": \"red\" }\n        ]\n      },\n      \"unit\": \"percent\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Daily Loss Budget Bar:**\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Daily Loss Budget\",\n  \"type\": \"bargauge\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_daily_loss_budget_remaining_pct\", \"legendFormat\": \"Budget Remaining\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"min\": 0, \"max\": 100,\n      \"thresholds\": {\n        \"steps\": [\n          { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"red\" },\n          { \"value\": 30, \"color\": \"orange\" },\n          { \"value\": 60, \"color\": \"yellow\" },\n          { \"value\": 80, \"color\": \"green\" }\n        ]\n      },\n      \"unit\": \"percent\"\n    }\n  },\n  \"options\": { \"orientation\": \"horizontal\", \"displayMode\": \"gradient\" }\n}\n```\n\n**Kill Switch Status Panel:**\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Kill Switch Status\",\n  \"type\": \"table\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    {\n      \"expr\": \"ep2_kill_switch_triggered\",\n      \"legendFormat\": \"{{switch_name}}\",\n      \"format\": \"table\",\n      \"instant\": true\n    }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"overrides\": [\n      {\n        \"matcher\": { \"id\": \"byName\", \"options\": \"Value\" },\n        \"properties\": [\n          {\n            \"id\": \"mappings\",\n            \"value\": [\n              { \"type\": \"value\", \"options\": { \"0\": { \"text\": \"ARMED\", \"color\": \"green\" } } },\n              { \"type\": \"value\", \"options\": { \"1\": { \"text\": \"TRIGGERED\", \"color\": \"red\" } } }\n            ]\n          }\n        ]\n      }\n    ]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Alerting Hierarchy\n\n### Prometheus Alert Rules\n\n```yaml\n# prometheus/rules/ep2_crypto_alerts.yml\n\ngroups:\n  - name: ep2_crypto_info\n    rules:\n      - alert: EP2PositionOpened\n        expr: ep2_position_side != 0 and changes(ep2_position_side[5m]) > 0\n        for: 0s\n        labels:\n          severity: info\n          channel: log_only\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Position opened\"\n          description: \"Side={{ $labels.symbol }} Quantity={{ $value }}\"\n\n      - alert: EP2TradeExecuted\n        expr: increase(ep2_trades_today_total[5m]) > 0\n        for: 0s\n        labels:\n          severity: info\n          channel: log_only\n\n  - name: ep2_crypto_warning\n    rules:\n      - alert: EP2DrawdownWarning\n        expr: ep2_drawdown_from_peak_pct > 3\n        for: 5m\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n          channel: telegram\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Drawdown exceeds 3%\"\n          description: \"Current drawdown: {{ $value | printf \\\"%.1f\\\" }}%\"\n\n      - alert: EP2ConsecutiveLossesWarning\n        expr: ep2_consecutive_losses > 5\n        for: 0s\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n          channel: telegram\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"{{ $value }} consecutive losing trades\"\n\n      - alert: EP2DailyLossBudgetLow\n        expr: ep2_daily_loss_budget_remaining_pct < 50\n        for: 5m\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n          channel: telegram\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Daily loss budget below 50%\"\n          description: \"Remaining: {{ $value | printf \\\"%.0f\\\" }}%\"\n\n      - alert: EP2SharpeDecay\n        expr: ep2_rolling_sharpe{window=\"7d\"} < 0.3\n        for: 30m\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n          channel: telegram\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"7d rolling Sharpe dropped below 0.3\"\n\n      - alert: EP2HighVolatility\n        expr: ep2_volatility_annualized > 1.2\n        for: 15m\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n          channel: telegram\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Annualized volatility {{ $value | printf \\\"%.0f\\\" }}% exceeds 120%\"\n\n  - name: ep2_crypto_critical\n    rules:\n      - alert: EP2DrawdownCritical\n        expr: ep2_drawdown_from_peak_pct > 10\n        for: 1m\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n          channel: telegram_discord\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"CRITICAL: Drawdown exceeds 10%\"\n          description: \"Drawdown: {{ $value | printf \\\"%.1f\\\" }}%. Halt threshold: 15%.\"\n\n      - alert: EP2DailyLossCritical\n        expr: ep2_daily_loss_budget_remaining_pct < 20\n        for: 1m\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n          channel: telegram_discord\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"CRITICAL: Daily loss budget nearly exhausted\"\n          description: \"Only {{ $value | printf \\\"%.0f\\\" }}% remaining\"\n\n      - alert: EP2ConsecutiveLossesCritical\n        expr: ep2_consecutive_losses > 10\n        for: 0s\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n          channel: telegram_discord\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"CRITICAL: {{ $value }} consecutive losses\"\n\n      - alert: EP2DrawdownGateHalted\n        expr: ep2_drawdown_gate_multiplier == 0\n        for: 0s\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n          channel: telegram_discord\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"CRITICAL: Drawdown gate halted all trading\"\n\n  - name: ep2_crypto_emergency\n    rules:\n      - alert: EP2KillSwitchTriggered\n        expr: ep2_kill_switch_triggered == 1\n        for: 0s\n        labels:\n          severity: emergency\n          channel: telegram_discord_sms\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"EMERGENCY: Kill switch {{ $labels.switch_name }} TRIGGERED\"\n          description: \"All trading halted. Manual intervention required.\"\n\n      - alert: EP2LiquidationRisk\n        expr: ep2_liquidation_distance_pct < 2\n        for: 0s\n        labels:\n          severity: emergency\n          channel: telegram_discord_sms\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"EMERGENCY: Liquidation distance < 2%\"\n          description: \"Distance to liquidation: {{ $value | printf \\\"%.2f\\\" }}%\"\n\n      - alert: EP2EmergencyDrawdown\n        expr: ep2_drawdown_from_peak_pct > 13\n        for: 0s\n        labels:\n          severity: emergency\n          channel: telegram_discord_sms\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"EMERGENCY: Drawdown {{ $value | printf \\\"%.1f\\\" }}% approaching 15% halt\"\n```\n\n### Notification Channel Configuration per Level\n\n| Level | `for` Duration | Channels | Repeat Interval |\n|-------|-----------|----------|-----------------|\n| INFO | 0s | Log only (no external notification) | N/A |\n| WARNING | 5m | Telegram bot | 30m |\n| CRITICAL | 1m | Telegram + Discord webhook | 10m |\n| EMERGENCY | 0s (instant) | Telegram + Discord + PagerDuty/SMS | 5m |\n\n### Alertmanager Config\n\n```yaml\n# alertmanager/alertmanager.yml\n\nglobal:\n  resolve_timeout: 5m\n\nroute:\n  receiver: \"default\"\n  routes:\n    - match:\n        channel: log_only\n      receiver: \"null_receiver\"\n\n    - match:\n        channel: telegram\n      receiver: \"telegram_bot\"\n      repeat_interval: 30m\n      group_wait: 10s\n\n    - match:\n        channel: telegram_discord\n      receiver: \"telegram_and_discord\"\n      repeat_interval: 10m\n      group_wait: 5s\n\n    - match:\n        channel: telegram_discord_sms\n      receiver: \"all_channels\"\n      repeat_interval: 5m\n      group_wait: 0s\n\nreceivers:\n  - name: \"default\"\n    webhook_configs: []\n\n  - name: \"null_receiver\"\n\n  - name: \"telegram_bot\"\n    telegram_configs:\n      - bot_token_file: \"/run/secrets/telegram_bot_token\"\n        chat_id: -1001234567890\n        parse_mode: \"HTML\"\n        message: |\n          <b>{{ .CommonLabels.alertname }}</b>\n          Severity: {{ .CommonLabels.severity }}\n          {{ range .Alerts }}{{ .Annotations.summary }}\n          {{ .Annotations.description }}{{ end }}\n\n  - name: \"telegram_and_discord\"\n    telegram_configs:\n      - bot_token_file: \"/run/secrets/telegram_bot_token\"\n        chat_id: -1001234567890\n        parse_mode: \"HTML\"\n    webhook_configs:\n      - url: \"https://discord.com/api/webhooks/YOUR_WEBHOOK_ID/YOUR_WEBHOOK_TOKEN\"\n        send_resolved: true\n\n  - name: \"all_channels\"\n    telegram_configs:\n      - bot_token_file: \"/run/secrets/telegram_bot_token\"\n        chat_id: -1001234567890\n    webhook_configs:\n      - url: \"https://discord.com/api/webhooks/YOUR_WEBHOOK_ID/YOUR_WEBHOOK_TOKEN\"\n    pagerduty_configs:\n      - routing_key_file: \"/run/secrets/pagerduty_routing_key\"\n        severity: critical\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Prometheus + Grafana Implementation\n\n### Prometheus Configuration\n\n```yaml\n# prometheus/prometheus.yml\n\nglobal:\n  scrape_interval: 15s      # Match to bar update frequency\n  evaluation_interval: 15s\n\nrule_files:\n  - \"rules/ep2_crypto_alerts.yml\"\n\nalerting:\n  alertmanagers:\n    - static_configs:\n        - targets: [\"alertmanager:9093\"]\n\nscrape_configs:\n  - job_name: \"ep2_crypto\"\n    metrics_path: \"/metrics\"\n    scrape_interval: 5s       # 5s for real-time position monitoring\n    static_configs:\n      - targets: [\"ep2-api:8000\"]\n        labels:\n          instance: \"live\"\n\n  - job_name: \"ep2_crypto_backtest\"\n    metrics_path: \"/metrics\"\n    scrape_interval: 30s\n    static_configs:\n      - targets: [\"ep2-backtest:8001\"]\n        labels:\n          instance: \"backtest\"\n```\n\n### FastAPI Metrics Endpoint\n\nThis integrates with the existing `api/server.py` slot:\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/api/metrics_endpoint.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter\nfrom prometheus_client import (\n    generate_latest,\n    CONTENT_TYPE_LATEST,\n)\nfrom starlette.responses import Response\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n\n@router.get(\"/metrics\")\nasync def metrics() -> Response:\n    \"\"\"Prometheus metrics endpoint.\n\n    Returns all registered Prometheus metrics in the exposition format.\n    Grafana/Prometheus scrapes this endpoint.\n    \"\"\"\n    return Response(\n        content=generate_latest(),\n        media_type=CONTENT_TYPE_LATEST,\n    )\n\n\n@router.get(\"/health\")\nasync def health() -> dict[str, str | bool | float]:\n    \"\"\"Health check that verifies actual dependencies.\n\n    Returns detailed status of each subsystem. Never returns 'ok'\n    without checking dependencies (per CLAUDE.md rules).\n    \"\"\"\n    # Import here to avoid circular imports at module level\n    import time\n\n    checks: dict[str, str | bool | float] = {\n        \"status\": \"healthy\",\n        \"timestamp\": time.time(),\n    }\n\n    # Each check should actually verify its dependency\n    # These will be filled in when the components exist\n    # checks[\"database\"] = _check_database()\n    # checks[\"exchange_ws\"] = _check_exchange_ws()\n    # checks[\"model_loaded\"] = _check_model()\n    # checks[\"last_prediction_age_s\"] = _check_prediction_freshness()\n\n    return checks\n```\n\n### Docker Compose (Full Stack)\n\n```yaml\n# docker/docker-compose.monitoring.yml\n\nservices:\n  prometheus:\n    image: prom/prometheus:v2.51.0\n    volumes:\n      - ../prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n      - ../prometheus/rules:/etc/prometheus/rules\n      - prometheus_data:/prometheus\n    ports:\n      - \"9090:9090\"\n    command:\n      - \"--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\"\n      - \"--storage.tsdb.retention.time=90d\"\n      - \"--web.enable-lifecycle\"\n\n  alertmanager:\n    image: prom/alertmanager:v0.27.0\n    volumes:\n      - ../alertmanager/alertmanager.yml:/etc/alertmanager/alertmanager.yml\n    ports:\n      - \"9093:9093\"\n\n  grafana:\n    image: grafana/grafana:11.0.0\n    volumes:\n      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana\n      - ../grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning\n      - ../grafana/dashboards:/var/lib/grafana/dashboards\n    ports:\n      - \"3000:3000\"\n    environment:\n      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD__FILE: /run/secrets/grafana_admin_pw\n      GF_DASHBOARDS_DEFAULT_HOME_DASHBOARD_PATH: /var/lib/grafana/dashboards/ep2_risk.json\n      GF_AUTH_ANONYMOUS_ENABLED: \"false\"\n\nvolumes:\n  prometheus_data:\n  grafana_data:\n```\n\n### Complete Metric Name Reference Table\n\n| Metric | Type | Labels | Update Frequency |\n|--------|------|--------|-----------------|\n| `ep2_position_side` | Gauge | symbol | Every bar |\n| `ep2_position_quantity_btc` | Gauge | symbol | Every bar |\n| `ep2_position_entry_price` | Gauge | symbol | On trade open |\n| `ep2_position_notional_usd` | Gauge | symbol | Every bar |\n| `ep2_position_unrealized_pnl_usd` | Gauge | symbol | Every bar |\n| `ep2_position_bars_held` | Gauge | symbol | Every bar |\n| `ep2_position_holding_duration_seconds` | Gauge | symbol | Every bar |\n| `ep2_stop_distance_pct` | Gauge | symbol | Every bar |\n| `ep2_liquidation_distance_pct` | Gauge | symbol | Every bar |\n| `ep2_daily_pnl_usd` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_weekly_pnl_usd` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_equity_usd` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_peak_equity_usd` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_drawdown_from_peak_pct` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_drawdown_gate_multiplier` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_margin_utilization_pct` | Gauge | symbol | Every bar |\n| `ep2_kill_switch_triggered` | Gauge | switch_name | Every bar |\n| `ep2_kill_switch_current_value` | Gauge | switch_name | Every bar |\n| `ep2_kill_switch_threshold` | Gauge | switch_name | On startup |\n| `ep2_trades_today_total` | Gauge | - | On trade |\n| `ep2_trades_total` | Counter | side, result | On trade close |\n| `ep2_consecutive_losses` | Gauge | - | On trade close |\n| `ep2_risk_state` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_daily_loss_budget_remaining_pct` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_volatility_annualized` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_volatility_state` | Gauge | - | Every bar |\n| `ep2_rolling_sharpe` | Gauge | window | Every 5m |\n| `ep2_rolling_win_rate` | Gauge | window | Every 5m |\n| `ep2_rolling_max_drawdown_pct` | Gauge | window | Every 5m |\n| `ep2_rolling_profit_factor` | Gauge | window | Every 5m |\n| `ep2_rolling_trades_per_day` | Gauge | window | Every 5m |\n| `ep2_rolling_avg_trade_pnl_usd` | Gauge | window | Every 5m |\n| `ep2_rolling_avg_trade_pnl_bps` | Gauge | window | Every 5m |\n\n---\n\n## 6. PnL Attribution on Dashboard\n\n### Prometheus Metrics\n\n```python\n# ── PnL Attribution ──\nep2_pnl_by_signal_source_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_pnl_by_signal_source_usd\",\n    \"Today's PnL attributed to each signal source\",\n    [\"source\"],  # \"microstructure\", \"cross_market\", \"regime\", \"ensemble\"\n)\nep2_pnl_by_direction_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_pnl_by_direction_usd\",\n    \"Today's PnL by trade direction\",\n    [\"direction\"],  # \"long\", \"short\"\n)\nep2_pnl_by_session_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_pnl_by_session_usd\",\n    \"Today's PnL by trading session\",\n    [\"session\"],  # \"asia\", \"europe\", \"us\"\n)\nep2_pnl_gross_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_pnl_gross_usd\",\n    \"Today's gross PnL (before fees)\",\n)\nep2_pnl_net_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_pnl_net_usd\",\n    \"Today's net PnL (after fees and slippage)\",\n)\nep2_pnl_fees_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_pnl_fees_usd\",\n    \"Total fees paid today\",\n)\nep2_pnl_slippage_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_pnl_slippage_usd\",\n    \"Total slippage cost today\",\n)\n```\n\n### PnL Attribution Tracker\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/pnl_attribution.py\n\nimport sqlite3\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\n\nimport structlog\n\nlogger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass TradeRecord:\n    \"\"\"Record of a completed trade with attribution metadata.\"\"\"\n    timestamp_ms: int\n    direction: str        # \"long\" or \"short\"\n    signal_source: str    # primary signal that triggered the trade\n    session: str          # \"asia\", \"europe\", \"us\"\n    gross_pnl: float      # PnL before costs\n    fees: float           # exchange fees\n    slippage: float       # estimated slippage\n    net_pnl: float        # gross - fees - slippage\n\n\ndef _classify_session(hour_utc: int) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Map UTC hour to trading session.\"\"\"\n    if 0 <= hour_utc < 8:\n        return \"asia\"\n    elif 8 <= hour_utc < 16:\n        return \"europe\"\n    else:\n        return \"us\"\n\n\nclass PnLAttributionTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks PnL broken down by signal source, direction, session, and costs.\n\n    Each time a trade closes, call `record_trade()` with the metadata.\n    Call `export_to_prometheus()` to push current day's attribution.\n\n    Why this matters: If all profits come from shorts during US session\n    but longs during Asia are losing, you know where the edge is and\n    can adjust the model or trading hours.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        self._today_trades: list[TradeRecord] = []\n        self._last_reset_date: str = \"\"\n\n    def record_trade(\n        self,\n        timestamp_ms: int,\n        direction: str,\n        signal_source: str,\n        gross_pnl: float,\n        fees: float,\n        slippage: float,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Record a closed trade for attribution.\"\"\"\n        dt = datetime.fromtimestamp(timestamp_ms / 1000, tz=timezone.utc)\n        session = _classify_session(dt.hour)\n        net_pnl = gross_pnl - fees - slippage\n\n        record = TradeRecord(\n            timestamp_ms=timestamp_ms,\n            direction=direction,\n            signal_source=signal_source,\n            session=session,\n            gross_pnl=gross_pnl,\n            fees=fees,\n            slippage=slippage,\n            net_pnl=net_pnl,\n        )\n        self._today_trades.append(record)\n\n        logger.info(\n            \"pnl_attribution_recorded\",\n            direction=direction,\n            source=signal_source,\n            session=session,\n            gross_pnl=round(gross_pnl, 2),\n            net_pnl=round(net_pnl, 2),\n        )\n\n    def reset_daily(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Call at 00:00 UTC to reset daily attribution.\"\"\"\n        self._today_trades = []\n\n    def export_to_prometheus(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Push current day's attribution to Prometheus gauges.\"\"\"\n        # By signal source\n        source_pnl: dict[str, float] = {}\n        direction_pnl: dict[str, float] = {}\n        session_pnl: dict[str, float] = {}\n        total_gross = 0.0\n        total_fees = 0.0\n        total_slippage = 0.0\n        total_net = 0.0\n\n        for t in self._today_trades:\n            source_pnl[t.signal_source] = source_pnl.get(t.signal_source, 0.0) + t.net_pnl\n            direction_pnl[t.direction] = direction_pnl.get(t.direction, 0.0) + t.net_pnl\n            session_pnl[t.session] = session_pnl.get(t.session, 0.0) + t.net_pnl\n            total_gross += t.gross_pnl\n            total_fees += t.fees\n            total_slippage += t.slippage\n            total_net += t.net_pnl\n\n        for source, pnl in source_pnl.items():\n            ep2_pnl_by_signal_source_usd.labels(source=source).set(pnl)\n        for direction, pnl in direction_pnl.items():\n            ep2_pnl_by_direction_usd.labels(direction=direction).set(pnl)\n        for session, pnl in session_pnl.items():\n            ep2_pnl_by_session_usd.labels(session=session).set(pnl)\n\n        ep2_pnl_gross_usd.set(total_gross)\n        ep2_pnl_net_usd.set(total_net)\n        ep2_pnl_fees_usd.set(total_fees)\n        ep2_pnl_slippage_usd.set(total_slippage)\n```\n\n### Grafana Panels (Row: PnL Attribution)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Today's PnL by Signal Source\",\n  \"type\": \"barchart\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_pnl_by_signal_source_usd\", \"legendFormat\": \"{{source}}\", \"format\": \"table\", \"instant\": true }\n  ],\n  \"options\": { \"orientation\": \"horizontal\", \"stacking\": \"none\" }\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Gross vs Net PnL\",\n  \"type\": \"stat\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_pnl_gross_usd\", \"legendFormat\": \"Gross\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_pnl_net_usd\", \"legendFormat\": \"Net\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_pnl_fees_usd\", \"legendFormat\": \"Fees\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_pnl_slippage_usd\", \"legendFormat\": \"Slippage\" }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Risk State History\n\n### Prometheus Metrics\n\nTime series data is automatically stored by Prometheus. The key is to expose the right gauges so Prometheus retains the history.\n\n```python\n# ── History metrics (exported every bar, Prometheus stores the time series) ──\nep2_equity_curve_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_equity_curve_usd\",\n    \"Equity at each bar (Prometheus stores history)\",\n)\nep2_position_size_history_btc = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_position_size_history_btc\",\n    \"Position size at each bar for position-over-time chart\",\n)\nep2_daily_pnl_bar_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_daily_pnl_bar_usd\",\n    \"Daily PnL for bar chart (reset each day)\",\n)\nep2_kill_switch_activation_total = Counter(\n    \"ep2_kill_switch_activation_total\",\n    \"Cumulative kill switch activations\",\n    [\"switch_name\"],\n)\n```\n\n### Grafana Panel Configuration (Row: History Charts)\n\n**Drawdown Over \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"custom\": {\n        \"fillOpacity\": 30,\n        \"lineWidth\": 1,\n        \"drawStyle\": \"line\",\n        \"fillBelowTo\": \"Threshold\"\n      },\n      \"color\": { \"mode\": \"fixed\", \"fixedColor\": \"red\" },\n      \"unit\": \"percent\"\n    }\n  },\n  \"options\": {\n    \"tooltip\": { \"mode\": \"single\" }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Equity
