  { \"expr\": \"ep2_peak_equity_usd\", \"legendFormat\": \"Peak\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"custom\": { \"lineWidth\": 2, \"fillOpacity\": 5 },\n      \"unit\": \"currencyUSD\"\n    },\n    \"overrides\": [\n      {\n        \"matcher\": { \"id\": \"byName\", \"options\": \"Peak\" },\n        \"properties\": [\n          { \"id\": \"custom.lineStyle\", \"value\": { \"fill\": \"dash\", \"dash\": [10, 10] } },\n          { \"id\": \"color\", \"value\": { \"fixedColor\": \"yellow\" } }\n        ]\n      }\n    ]\n  }\n}\n```\n\nTo annotate kill switch activations on the equity curve, use Grafana's annotation feature with a Prometheus query:\n\n```\nAnnotation query: increase(ep2_kill_switch_activation_total[1m]) > 0\nTags: kill_switch\nColor: red\n```\n\n**Position Size Over Time:**\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Position Size Over Time\",\n  \"type\": \"timeseries\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_position_quantity_btc{symbol=\\\"BTCUSDT\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Size BTC\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"custom\": { \"drawStyle\": \"bars\", \"fillOpacity\": 80 },\n      \"unit\": \"BTC\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Daily PnL Bars:**\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Daily PnL\",\n  \"type\": \"barchart\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    {\n      \"expr\": \"max_over_time(ep2_daily_pnl_usd[1d])\",\n      \"legendFormat\": \"Daily PnL\",\n      \"interval\": \"1d\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"custom\": { \"fillOpacity\": 80 },\n      \"thresholds\": {\n        \"steps\": [\n          { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"red\" },\n          { \"value\": 0, \"color\": \"green\" }\n        ]\n      },\n      \"unit\": \"currencyUSD\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Model Health on Risk Dashboard\n\n### Prometheus Metrics\n\n```python\n# ── Model health ──\nep2_model_accuracy_rolling = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_model_accuracy_rolling\",\n    \"Rolling directional accuracy\",\n    [\"model\", \"window\"],  # model: \"lgbm\", \"catboost\", \"ensemble\"; window: \"7d\"\n)\nep2_model_predictions_total = Counter(\n    \"ep2_model_predictions_total\",\n    \"Total predictions made\",\n    [\"model\", \"predicted_class\"],  # \"up\", \"down\", \"flat\"\n)\nep2_feature_drift_psi = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_feature_drift_psi\",\n    \"Population Stability Index for feature drift\",\n    [\"feature_name\"],\n)\nep2_feature_drift_alert = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_feature_drift_alert\",\n    \"1 if PSI > 0.2 (significant drift), 0 otherwise\",\n    [\"feature_name\"],\n)\nep2_prediction_confidence_mean = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_prediction_confidence_mean\",\n    \"Mean confidence of predictions in recent window\",\n    [\"model\"],\n)\nep2_prediction_confidence_histogram = Histogram(\n    \"ep2_prediction_confidence_histogram\",\n    \"Distribution of prediction confidence scores\",\n    [\"model\"],\n    buckets=[0.5, 0.55, 0.6, 0.65, 0.7, 0.75, 0.8, 0.85, 0.9, 0.95, 1.0],\n)\nep2_prediction_distribution = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_prediction_distribution\",\n    \"Fraction of predictions in each class\",\n    [\"model\", \"predicted_class\"],\n)\n```\n\n### Model Health Monitor\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/model_health.py\n\nfrom collections import deque\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport structlog\n\nlogger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass PredictionRecord:\n    timestamp_ms: int\n    model: str\n    predicted_class: str  # \"up\", \"down\", \"flat\"\n    confidence: float\n    actual_class: str | None = None  # filled in after outcome is known\n\n\nclass ModelHealthMonitor:\n    \"\"\"Tracks model prediction quality and feature drift.\n\n    Maintains a rolling buffer of predictions and their outcomes.\n    Computes accuracy, confidence distributions, and checks for\n    distributional drift.\n\n    PSI (Population Stability Index) thresholds:\n        PSI < 0.1:  No significant drift\n        PSI 0.1-0.2: Moderate drift, monitor closely\n        PSI > 0.2:  Significant drift, trigger retraining\n\n    These thresholds are standard in credit scoring and apply well\n    to feature distributions in trading models.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, max_buffer_size: int = 5000) -> None:\n        self._buffer: deque[PredictionRecord] = deque(maxlen=max_buffer_size)\n        self._reference_distributions: dict[str, np.ndarray] = {}\n\n    def record_prediction(\n        self,\n        timestamp_ms: int,\n        model: str,\n        predicted_class: str,\n        confidence: float,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Record a new prediction.\"\"\"\n        record = PredictionRecord(\n            timestamp_ms=timestamp_ms,\n            model=model,\n            predicted_class=predicted_class,\n            confidence=confidence,\n        )\n        self._buffer.append(record)\n\n        # Update Prometheus\n        ep2_model_predictions_total.labels(\n            model=model, predicted_class=predicted_class\n        ).inc()\n        ep2_prediction_confidence_histogram.labels(model=model).observe(confidence)\n\n    def record_outcome(self, timestamp_ms: int, actual_class: str) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Record the actual outcome for a previous prediction.\n\n        Matches by timestamp (within 5-min bar tolerance).\n        \"\"\"\n        tolerance_ms = 5 * 60 * 1000  # 5 min\n        for record in reversed(self._buffer):\n            if abs(record.timestamp_ms - timestamp_ms) < tolerance_ms and record.actual_class is None:\n                record.actual_class = actual_class\n                break\n\n    def set_reference_distribution(\n        self, feature_name: str, distribution: np.ndarray\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Set the reference (training) distribution for PSI comparison.\"\"\"\n        self._reference_distributions[feature_name] = distribution\n\n    def compute_psi(\n        self, feature_name: str, current_values: np.ndarray, n_bins: int = 10\n    ) -> float:\n        \"\"\"Compute Population Stability Index between reference and current.\n\n        PSI = SUM( (actual_pct - expected_pct) * ln(actual_pct / expected_pct) )\n\n        Args:\n            feature_name: Name of the feature being checked.\n            current_values: Current period's feature values.\n            n_bins: Number of bins for discretization.\n\n        Returns:\n            PSI value. > 0.2 indicates significant drift.\n        \"\"\"\n        if feature_name not in self._reference_distributions:\n            return 0.0\n\n        reference = self._reference_distributions[feature_name]\n        if len(reference) == 0 or len(current_values) == 0:\n            return 0.0\n\n        # Create bins from reference distribution\n        breakpoints = np.percentile(reference, np.linspace(0, 100, n_bins + 1))\n        breakpoints[0] = -np.inf\n        breakpoints[-1] = np.inf\n\n        # Count in each bin\n        expected_counts = np.histogram(reference, bins=breakpoints)[0]\n        actual_counts = np.histogram(current_values, bins=breakpoints)[0]\n\n        # Convert to proportions (with smoothing to avoid log(0))\n        expected_pct = (expected_counts + 1) / (len(reference) + n_bins)\n        actual_pct = (actual_counts + 1) / (len(current_values) + n_bins)\n\n        psi = float(np.sum((actual_pct - expected_pct) * np.log(actual_pct / expected_pct)))\n\n        # Export to Prometheus\n        ep2_feature_drift_psi.labels(feature_name=feature_name).set(psi)\n        ep2_feature_drift_alert.labels(feature_name=feature_name).set(\n            1.0 if psi > 0.2 else 0.0\n        )\n\n        if psi > 0.2:\n            logger.warning(\n                \"feature_drift_detected\",\n                feature=feature_name,\n                psi=round(psi, 4),\n            )\n\n        return psi\n\n    def export_accuracy_to_prometheus(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Compute and export rolling accuracy for each model.\"\"\"\n        import time\n        now_ms = int(time.time() * 1000)\n        seven_days_ms = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000\n\n        # Group by model\n        model_records: dict[str, list[PredictionRecord]] = {}\n        for r in self._buffer:\n            if r.actual_class is not None and (now_ms - r.timestamp_ms) < seven_days_ms:\n                model_records.setdefault(r.model, []).append(r)\n\n        for model, records in model_records.items():\n            if not records:\n                continue\n\n            correct = sum(1 for r in records if r.predicted_class == r.actual_class)\n            accuracy = correct / len(records)\n            ep2_model_accuracy_rolling.labels(model=model, window=\"7d\").set(accuracy)\n\n            # Confidence distribution\n            confidences = [r.confidence for r in records]\n            ep2_prediction_confidence_mean.labels(model=model).set(\n                float(np.mean(confidences))\n            )\n\n            # Prediction class distribution\n            total = len(records)\n            for cls in (\"up\", \"down\", \"flat\"):\n                count = sum(1 for r in records if r.predicted_class == cls)\n                ep2_prediction_distribution.labels(\n                    model=model, predicted_class=cls\n                ).set(count / total)\n```\n\n### Grafana Panels (Row: Model Health)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Model Accuracy (7d Rolling)\",\n  \"type\": \"stat\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_model_accuracy_rolling{window=\\\"7d\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"{{model}}\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"unit\": \"percentunit\",\n      \"thresholds\": {\n        \"steps\": [\n          { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"red\" },\n          { \"value\": 0.50, \"color\": \"yellow\" },\n          { \"value\": 0.53, \"color\": \"green\" }\n        ]\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Feature Drift (PSI)\",\n  \"type\": \"table\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"topk(10, ep2_feature_drift_psi)\", \"legendFormat\": \"{{feature_name}}\", \"format\": \"table\", \"instant\": true }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"overrides\": [\n      {\n        \"matcher\": { \"id\": \"byName\", \"options\": \"Value\" },\n        \"properties\": [\n          {\n            \"id\": \"thresholds\",\n            \"value\": {\n              \"steps\": [\n                { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"green\" },\n                { \"value\": 0.1, \"color\": \"yellow\" },\n                { \"value\": 0.2, \"color\": \"red\" }\n              ]\n            }\n          }\n        ]\n      }\n    ]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Alert Rules for Model Health\n\n```yaml\n# Added to prometheus/rules/ep2_crypto_alerts.yml\n\n  - name: ep2_model_health\n    rules:\n      - alert: EP2ModelAccuracyDegraded\n        expr: ep2_model_accuracy_rolling{window=\"7d\"} < 0.50\n        for: 1h\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n          channel: telegram_discord\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Model {{ $labels.model }} accuracy below 50%\"\n          description: \"7d accuracy: {{ $value | printf \\\"%.1f\\\" }}%. Worse than random. Consider retraining.\"\n\n      - alert: EP2FeatureDriftDetected\n        expr: ep2_feature_drift_alert == 1\n        for: 30m\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n          channel: telegram\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Feature drift detected: {{ $labels.feature_name }}\"\n          description: \"PSI > 0.2 for 30 minutes. Model inputs may have shifted.\"\n\n      - alert: EP2PredictionDistributionSkewed\n        expr: ep2_prediction_distribution{predicted_class=\"flat\"} > 0.8\n        for: 2h\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n          channel: telegram\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Model predicting 'flat' >80% of the time\"\n          description: \"The model may be undertrained or the market regime has shifted.\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Execution Quality Metrics\n\n### Prometheus Metrics\n\n```python\n# ── Execution quality ──\nep2_slippage_bps = Histogram(\n    \"ep2_slippage_bps\",\n    \"Slippage per trade in basis points\",\n    [\"side\"],\n    buckets=[0, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, 10, 15, 20, 30, 50],\n)\nep2_slippage_avg_bps = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_slippage_avg_bps\",\n    \"Average slippage over rolling window in basis points\",\n    [\"window\"],\n)\nep2_fill_rate_pct = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_fill_rate_pct\",\n    \"Percentage of orders that were filled (vs cancelled/expired)\",\n)\nep2_order_latency_ms = Histogram(\n    \"ep2_order_latency_ms\",\n    \"Latency from signal to fill in milliseconds\",\n    buckets=[50, 100, 200, 300, 500, 750, 1000, 2000, 5000],\n)\nep2_order_latency_avg_ms = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_order_latency_avg_ms\",\n    \"Average order latency in milliseconds\",\n)\nep2_failed_orders_total = Counter(\n    \"ep2_failed_orders_total\",\n    \"Cumulative count of failed/rejected orders\",\n    [\"reason\"],  # \"insufficient_margin\", \"rate_limit\", \"network\", \"exchange_error\"\n)\nep2_orders_total = Counter(\n    \"ep2_orders_total\",\n    \"Total orders submitted\",\n    [\"status\"],  # \"filled\", \"partial\", \"cancelled\", \"failed\"\n)\n```\n\n### Execution Quality Tracker\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/execution_quality.py\n\nfrom collections import deque\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport structlog\n\nlogger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass OrderRecord:\n    signal_time_ms: int\n    submit_time_ms: int\n    fill_time_ms: int | None\n    expected_price: float\n    fill_price: float | None\n    side: str\n    status: str  # \"filled\", \"partial\", \"cancelled\", \"failed\"\n    fail_reason: str | None = None\n\n\nclass ExecutionQualityTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks order execution quality: slippage, latency, fill rate.\n\n    For a 5-min BTC system with 8-12 bps round-trip cost assumption,\n    monitoring actual slippage is critical. If average slippage exceeds\n    5 bps consistently, the cost model in backtesting needs updating\n    and the effective Sharpe will be lower than backtested.\n\n    Call `record_order()` for every order submitted.\n    Call `export_to_prometheus()` periodically.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, max_buffer: int = 2000) -> None:\n        self._buffer: deque[OrderRecord] = deque(maxlen=max_buffer)\n\n    def record_order(self, order: OrderRecord) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Record an order for quality tracking.\"\"\"\n        self._buffer.append(order)\n\n        # Immediate Prometheus updates\n        ep2_orders_total.labels(status=order.status).inc()\n\n        if order.status == \"filled\" and order.fill_price is not None and order.fill_time_ms is not None:\n            # Slippage\n            if order.expected_price > 0:\n                slippage_bps = abs(order.fill_price - order.expected_price) / order.expected_price * 10000\n                ep2_slippage_bps.labels(side=order.side).observe(slippage_bps)\n\n            # Latency\n            latency = order.fill_time_ms - order.signal_time_ms\n            ep2_order_latency_ms.observe(latency)\n\n        elif order.status == \"failed\" and order.fail_reason:\n            ep2_failed_orders_total.labels(reason=order.fail_reason).inc()\n\n    def export_to_prometheus(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Compute and export aggregate execution quality metrics.\"\"\"\n        filled = [o for o in self._buffer if o.status == \"filled\"]\n        total = len(self._buffer)\n\n        if total > 0:\n            fill_rate = len(filled) / total * 100\n            ep2_fill_rate_pct.set(fill_rate)\n\n        if filled:\n            slippages = []\n            latencies = []\n            for o in filled:\n                if o.fill_price and o.expected_price > 0:\n                    s = abs(o.fill_price - o.expected_price) / o.expected_price * 10000\n                    slippages.append(s)\n                if o.fill_time_ms and o.signal_time_ms:\n                    latencies.append(o.fill_time_ms - o.signal_time_ms)\n\n            if slippages:\n                ep2_slippage_avg_bps.labels(window=\"all\").set(float(np.mean(slippages)))\n            if latencies:\n                ep2_order_latency_avg_ms.set(float(np.mean(latencies)))\n```\n\n### Grafana Panels (Row: Execution Quality)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Slippage Distribution\",\n  \"type\": \"histogram\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"rate(ep2_slippage_bps_bucket[1h])\", \"legendFormat\": \"{{le}} bps\" }\n  ],\n  \"options\": { \"bucketSize\": \"auto\" }\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Order Latency (p50/p95/p99)\",\n  \"type\": \"timeseries\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"histogram_quantile(0.50, rate(ep2_order_latency_ms_bucket[5m]))\", \"legendFormat\": \"p50\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"histogram_quantile(0.95, rate(ep2_order_latency_ms_bucket[5m]))\", \"legendFormat\": \"p95\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"histogram_quantile(0.99, rate(ep2_order_latency_ms_bucket[5m]))\", \"legendFormat\": \"p99\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": { \"defaults\": { \"unit\": \"ms\" } }\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Execution Stats\",\n  \"type\": \"stat\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_fill_rate_pct\", \"legendFormat\": \"Fill Rate\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_slippage_avg_bps{window=\\\"all\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Avg Slippage (bps)\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_order_latency_avg_ms\", \"legendFormat\": \"Avg Latency (ms)\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"rate(ep2_failed_orders_total[1h])\", \"legendFormat\": \"Failed Orders/hr\" }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Comparison Panel (System vs Benchmarks)\n\n### Prometheus Metrics\n\n```python\n# ── Benchmark comparison ──\nep2_benchmark_return_pct = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_benchmark_return_pct\",\n    \"Benchmark cumulative return for comparison\",\n    [\"benchmark\"],  # \"buy_hold\", \"btc_spot\", \"sp500\"\n)\nep2_system_return_pct = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_system_return_pct\",\n    \"System cumulative return\",\n)\nep2_system_vs_backtest_sharpe = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_system_vs_backtest_sharpe\",\n    \"Comparison of live vs backtest Sharpe\",\n    [\"source\"],  # \"live\", \"backtest\"\n)\nep2_system_vs_backtest_win_rate = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_system_vs_backtest_win_rate\",\n    \"Comparison of live vs backtest win rate\",\n    [\"source\"],\n)\nep2_today_vs_expected_pnl_usd = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_today_vs_expected_pnl_usd\",\n    \"Today's PnL vs backtest expected daily PnL\",\n    [\"series\"],  # \"actual\", \"expected\"\n)\n```\n\n### Benchmark Tracker\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/benchmark_tracker.py\n\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport structlog\n\nlogger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass BacktestExpectations:\n    \"\"\"Expected performance from the most recent backtest run.\n\n    Load these from the backtest results file/database at startup.\n    The dashboard shows live performance relative to these expectations\n    to detect live-vs-backtest divergence early.\n    \"\"\"\n    sharpe: float = 2.0       # Target from CLAUDE.md\n    win_rate: float = 0.54\n    avg_daily_pnl_usd: float = 50.0\n    max_drawdown_pct: float = 8.0\n    profit_factor: float = 1.3\n    avg_trades_per_day: float = 15.0\n\n\nclass BenchmarkTracker:\n    \"\"\"Tracks buy-and-hold and other benchmarks for comparison.\n\n    The key insight: if the system underperforms buy-and-hold over\n    a 30-day window, something is wrong. Either alpha has decayed,\n    costs are higher than modeled, or there is a bug.\n\n    This tracker also compares live Sharpe to backtest Sharpe.\n    Per CLAUDE.md, expect 50-70% degradation. If degradation exceeds\n    80%, the model needs investigation.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        initial_equity: float,\n        initial_btc_price: float,\n        backtest_expectations: BacktestExpectations | None = None,\n    ) -> None:\n        self._initial_equity = initial_equity\n        self._initial_btc_price = initial_btc_price\n        self._expectations = backtest_expectations or BacktestExpectations()\n\n    def export_to_prometheus(\n        self,\n        current_equity: float,\n        current_btc_price: float,\n        live_sharpe_30d: float,\n        live_win_rate_30d: float,\n        today_pnl: float,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Export benchmark comparisons.\"\"\"\n        # System return\n        sys_return = (current_equity - self._initial_equity) / self._initial_equity * 100\n        ep2_system_return_pct.set(sys_return)\n\n        # Buy and hold return\n        bh_return = (current_btc_price - self._initial_btc_price) / self._initial_btc_price * 100\n        ep2_benchmark_return_pct.labels(benchmark=\"buy_hold\").set(bh_return)\n\n        # Live vs backtest Sharpe\n        ep2_system_vs_backtest_sharpe.labels(source=\"live\").set(live_sharpe_30d)\n        ep2_system_vs_backtest_sharpe.labels(source=\"backtest\").set(self._expectations.sharpe)\n\n        # Live vs backtest win rate\n        ep2_system_vs_backtest_win_rate.labels(source=\"live\").set(live_win_rate_30d)\n        ep2_system_vs_backtest_win_rate.labels(source=\"backtest\").set(self._expectations.win_rate)\n\n        # Today vs expected\n        ep2_today_vs_expected_pnl_usd.labels(series=\"actual\").set(today_pnl)\n        ep2_today_vs_expected_pnl_usd.labels(series=\"expected\").set(\n            self._expectations.avg_daily_pnl_usd\n        )\n```\n\n### Grafana Panels (Row: Comparison)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"System vs Buy-and-Hold\",\n  \"type\": \"timeseries\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_system_return_pct\", \"legendFormat\": \"System\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_benchmark_return_pct{benchmark=\\\"buy_hold\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Buy & Hold\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": { \"defaults\": { \"unit\": \"percent\" } }\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Live vs Backtest Sharpe\",\n  \"type\": \"bargauge\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_system_vs_backtest_sharpe{source=\\\"live\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Live\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_system_vs_backtest_sharpe{source=\\\"backtest\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Backtest\" }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"thresholds\": {\n        \"steps\": [\n          { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"red\" },\n          { \"value\": 0.5, \"color\": \"yellow\" },\n          { \"value\": 1.0, \"color\": \"green\" }\n        ]\n      }\n    }\n  },\n  \"options\": { \"orientation\": \"horizontal\" }\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Today: Actual vs Expected PnL\",\n  \"type\": \"stat\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_today_vs_expected_pnl_usd{series=\\\"actual\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Actual\" },\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_today_vs_expected_pnl_usd{series=\\\"expected\\\"}\", \"legendFormat\": \"Expected\" }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Alert for Live-vs-Backtest Divergence\n\n```yaml\n      - alert: EP2LiveVsBacktestDivergence\n        expr: |\n          ep2_system_vs_backtest_sharpe{source=\"live\"}\n          / on() ep2_system_vs_backtest_sharpe{source=\"backtest\"}\n          < 0.2\n        for: 7d\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n          channel: telegram_discord\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Live Sharpe is <20% of backtest Sharpe for 7 days\"\n          description: \"Expected 50-70% degradation per CLAUDE.md. >80% degradation indicates model failure.\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 11. Mobile-Friendly Monitoring\n\n### Grafana Mobile Setup\n\nGrafana's responsive design works on mobile browsers, but for the best mobile experience:\n\n1. **Create a separate \"Mobile\" dashboard** with only the most critical panels in a single-column layout:\n   - Risk state traffic light (row 1)\n   - Equity + PnL stat (row 2)\n   - Drawdown gauge (row 3)\n   - Kill switch status (row 4)\n\n2. **Grafana Cloud or VPN**: Access over Tailscale/WireGuard VPN rather than exposing port 3000 to the internet.\n\n### Push Notifications via Telegram Bot\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/notifications.py\n\nimport httpx\nimport structlog\n\nlogger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n\n\nclass TelegramNotifier:\n    \"\"\"Sends formatted risk notifications to a Telegram chat.\n\n    This is used for direct notifications from Python (in addition\n    to Alertmanager). Useful for:\n        - Trade open/close confirmations\n        - Daily summary reports\n        - Custom formatted messages that Alertmanager cannot do\n\n    The bot token and chat_id come from environment variables,\n    never hardcoded.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, bot_token: str, chat_id: str) -> None:\n        self._bot_token = bot_token\n        self._chat_id = chat_id\n        self._base_url = f\"https://api.telegram.org/bot{bot_token}\"\n\n    async def send_message(self, text: str, parse_mode: str = \"HTML\") -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Send a message to the configured Telegram chat.\n\n        Returns True if sent successfully.\n        \"\"\"\n        try:\n            async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=10.0) as client:\n                resp = await client.post(\n                    f\"{self._base_url}/sendMessage\",\n                    json={\n                        \"chat_id\": self._chat_id,\n                        \"text\": text,\n                        \"parse_mode\": parse_mode,\n                    },\n                )\n                if resp.status_code != 200:\n                    logger.error(\n                        \"telegram_send_failed\",\n                        status_code=resp.status_code,\n                        response=resp.text[:200],\n                    )\n                    return False\n                return True\n        except Exception:\n            logger.exception(\"telegram_send_error\")\n            return False\n\n    async def send_risk_summary(\n        self,\n        equity: float,\n        daily_pnl: float,\n        drawdown_pct: float,\n        risk_level: str,\n        trades_today: int,\n        sharpe_7d: float,\n    ) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Send a formatted daily risk summary.\"\"\"\n        pnl_emoji_map = {\"GREEN\": \"OK\", \"YELLOW\": \"CAUTION\", \"RED\": \"DANGER\", \"EMERGENCY\": \"HALT\"}\n        status_label = pnl_emoji_map.get(risk_level, risk_level)\n\n        text = (\n            f\"<b>ep2-crypto Risk Summary</b>\\n\"\n            f\"<b>Status:</b> {status_label}\\n\\n\"\n            f\"Equity: ${equity:,.2f}\\n\"\n            f\"Daily PnL: ${daily_pnl:+,.2f}\\n\"\n            f\"Drawdown: {drawdown_pct:.1f}%\\n\"\n            f\"Trades today: {trades_today}\\n\"\n            f\"7d Sharpe: {sharpe_7d:.2f}\\n\"\n        )\n        return await self.send_message(text)\n\n\nclass DiscordNotifier:\n    \"\"\"Sends notifications to a Discord webhook.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, webhook_url: str) -> None:\n        self._webhook_url = webhook_url\n\n    async def send_message(self, content: str) -> bool:\n        try:\n            async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=10.0) as client:\n                resp = await client.post(\n                    self._webhook_url,\n                    json={\"content\": content},\n                )\n                return resp.status_code in (200, 204)\n        except Exception:\n            logger.exception(\"discord_send_error\")\n            return False\n```\n\n### Simple Status API Endpoint\n\n```python\n# Added to src/ep2_crypto/api/metrics_endpoint.py\n\n@router.get(\"/status\")\nasync def simple_status() -> dict[str, object]:\n    \"\"\"Minimal status endpoint for mobile/simple clients.\n\n    Returns a JSON blob with the most critical metrics.\n    Designed to be polled by a simple mobile app, curl script,\n    or Shortcuts automation on iOS.\n\n    Response shape:\n    {\n        \"risk_level\": \"GREEN\",\n        \"equity\": 50123.45,\n        \"daily_pnl\": -45.20,\n        \"drawdown_pct\": 1.2,\n        \"position\": \"flat\",\n        \"trades_today\": 8,\n        \"kill_switches_active\": [],\n        \"sharpe_7d\": 1.05\n    }\n    \"\"\"\n    # This will be populated from the RiskManager when integrated\n    return {\n        \"risk_level\": \"GREEN\",\n        \"equity\": 0.0,\n        \"daily_pnl\": 0.0,\n        \"drawdown_pct\": 0.0,\n        \"position\": \"flat\",\n        \"trades_today\": 0,\n        \"kill_switches_active\": [],\n        \"sharpe_7d\": 0.0,\n    }\n```\n\n---\n\n## 12. Dashboard for Backtesting vs Live\n\n### Architecture: Same Layout, Different Data Source\n\nThe key principle: the backtest engine and the live system expose the **exact same Prometheus metrics** under different job labels. In Prometheus config (shown in section 5), the live system scrapes from port 8000 with `instance: \"live\"` and the backtest from port 8001 with `instance: \"backtest\"`.\n\nIn Grafana, use a **template variable** `$instance` with values `live` and `backtest`. Every panel query uses `{instance=\"$instance\"}`:\n\n```\nep2_equity_usd{instance=\"$instance\"}\nep2_drawdown_from_peak_pct{instance=\"$instance\"}\nep2_rolling_sharpe{instance=\"$instance\", window=\"7d\"}\n```\n\nThis means one dashboard definition works for both modes.\n\n### Backtest-Only Additional Metrics\n\n```python\n# ── Backtest-specific metrics ──\nep2_backtest_fold_sharpe = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_backtest_fold_sharpe\",\n    \"Sharpe ratio for each walk-forward fold\",\n    [\"fold_id\"],\n)\nep2_backtest_fold_win_rate = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_backtest_fold_win_rate\",\n    \"Win rate for each walk-forward fold\",\n    [\"fold_id\"],\n)\nep2_backtest_fold_trades = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_backtest_fold_trades\",\n    \"Number of trades in each fold\",\n    [\"fold_id\"],\n)\nep2_backtest_cost_breakdown_bps = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_backtest_cost_breakdown_bps\",\n    \"Cost breakdown per component in basis points\",\n    [\"component\"],  # \"exchange_fee\", \"slippage\", \"funding\", \"spread\"\n)\nep2_backtest_gross_sharpe = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_backtest_gross_sharpe\",\n    \"Sharpe ratio before transaction costs\",\n)\nep2_backtest_net_sharpe = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_backtest_net_sharpe\",\n    \"Sharpe ratio after all transaction costs\",\n)\nep2_backtest_cost_drag_pct = Gauge(\n    \"ep2_backtest_cost_drag_pct\",\n    \"Percentage of gross returns consumed by costs\",\n)\n```\n\n### Backtest Metrics Exporter\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/monitoring/backtest_exporter.py\n\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport structlog\n\nlogger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass FoldResult:\n    fold_id: int\n    sharpe: float\n    win_rate: float\n    total_trades: int\n    gross_pnl: float\n    net_pnl: float\n    fees_paid: float\n    slippage_cost: float\n    funding_cost: float\n    spread_cost: float\n\n\nclass BacktestMetricsExporter:\n    \"\"\"Exports walk-forward backtest results to Prometheus.\n\n    Run this during or after a backtest to populate the same dashboard\n    with backtest data. The dashboard uses the `instance` label to\n    differentiate live vs backtest.\n\n    Per-fold Sharpe is critical: if fold-to-fold Sharpe variance is\n    high (std > 0.5 across folds), the strategy may be overfit to\n    certain regimes and will degrade in live trading.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def export_fold_results(self, folds: list[FoldResult]) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Export per-fold metrics.\"\"\"\n        total_gross = 0.0\n        total_net = 0.0\n        total_fees = 0.0\n        total_slippage = 0.0\n        total_funding = 0.0\n        total_spread = 0.0\n\n        for fold in folds:\n            ep2_backtest_fold_sharpe.labels(fold_id=str(fold.fold_id)).set(fold.sharpe)\n            ep2_backtest_fold_win_rate.labels(fold_id=str(fold.fold_id)).set(fold.win_rate)\n            ep2_backtest_fold_trades.labels(fold_id=str(fold.fold_id)).set(fold.total_trades)\n\n            total_gross += fold.gross_pnl\n            total_net += fold.net_pnl\n            total_fees += fold.fees_paid\n            total_slippage += fold.slippage_cost\n            total_funding += fold.funding_cost\n            total_spread += fold.spread_cost\n\n        # Cost breakdown\n        total_trades = sum(f.total_trades for f in folds)\n        if total_trades > 0:\n            avg_notional = 50000  # approximate per CLAUDE.md\n            ep2_backtest_cost_breakdown_bps.labels(component=\"exchange_fee\").set(\n                total_fees / (total_trades * avg_notional) * 10000\n            )\n            ep2_backtest_cost_breakdown_bps.labels(component=\"slippage\").set(\n                total_slippage / (total_trades * avg_notional) * 10000\n            )\n            ep2_backtest_cost_breakdown_bps.labels(component=\"funding\").set(\n                total_funding / (total_trades * avg_notional) * 10000\n            )\n            ep2_backtest_cost_breakdown_bps.labels(component=\"spread\").set(\n                total_spread / (total_trades * avg_notional) * 10000\n            )\n\n        # Gross vs net Sharpe\n        sharpes = [f.sharpe for f in folds]\n        if sharpes:\n            ep2_backtest_gross_sharpe.set(float(np.mean(sharpes)))\n            # Net Sharpe approximation\n            cost_drag = (total_gross - total_net) / abs(total_gross) * 100 if total_gross != 0 else 0\n            ep2_backtest_cost_drag_pct.set(cost_drag)\n\n        logger.info(\n            \"backtest_metrics_exported\",\n            folds=len(folds),\n            total_trades=total_trades,\n            cost_drag_pct=round(cost_drag if total_gross != 0 else 0, 2),\n        )\n```\n\n### Grafana Panels (Backtest-Only, Conditional Row)\n\nThese panels are conditionally shown when `$instance == \"backtest\"`:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Per-Fold Sharpe\",\n  \"type\": \"barchart\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_backtest_fold_sharpe\", \"legendFormat\": \"Fold {{fold_id}}\", \"format\": \"table\", \"instant\": true }\n  ],\n  \"fieldConfig\": {\n    \"defaults\": {\n      \"thresholds\": {\n        \"steps\": [\n          { \"value\": null, \"color\": \"red\" },\n          { \"value\": 1.0, \"color\": \"yellow\" },\n          { \"value\": 2.0, \"color\": \"green\" }\n        ]\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"title\": \"Cost Breakdown (bps per trade)\",\n  \"type\": \"piechart\",\n  \"targets\": [\n    { \"expr\": \"ep2_backtest_cost_breakdown_bps\", \"legendFormat\": \"{{component}}\", \"format\": \"table\", \"instant\": true }\n  ],\n  \"options\": { \"pieType\": \"donut\", \"displayLabels\": [\"name\", \"value\"] }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary: Complete Dashboard Layout\n\nThe Grafana dashboard is organized in **8 rows**, top to bottom, from most urgent to most analytical:\n\n| Row | Name | Key Panels | Update Rate |\n|-----|------|-----------|-------------|\n| 1 | **System Status** | Traffic light, kill switch table, drawdown gauge, daily loss budget bar | Every bar (5s scrape) |\n| 2 | **Position** | Side/size/entry stat, stop distance gauge, unrealized PnL, holding time | Every bar |\n| 3 | **PnL** | Equity curve (time series), daily PnL bars, gross vs net stat | Every bar |\n| 4 | **Rolling Performance** | 7d/30d Sharpe (time series), win rate, profit factor, trades/day (table) | Every 5 min |\n| 5 | **PnL Attribution** | By source (bar), by direction (bar), by session (bar), cost breakdown (stat) | Every 5 min |\n| 6 | **Model Health** | Accuracy stat, PSI table, confidence histogram, prediction distribution | Every 5 min |\n| 7 | **Execution Quality** | Slippage histogram, latency p50/p95/p99, fill rate, failed orders | On trade |\n| 8 | **Comparison** | System vs buy-hold (time series), live vs backtest Sharpe (bar gauge), today vs expected | Every 5 min |\n| 9 | **Backtest Only** | Per-fold Sharpe (bar), cost breakdown (pie) -- hidden in live mode | After backtest |\n\nTotal Prometheus metrics: **49 unique metric names** covering all 12 research areas. All use the `ep2_` prefix, parameterized queries, and structured logging per the project conventions."}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":5018,"cache_read_input_tokens":57840,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":5018,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"}},"requestId":"req_011CZL7vMvdvd6ynxNVFf58T","type":"assistant","uuid":"8cac38fb-677b-40d6-aa8b-d3e495561910","timestamp":"2026-03-23T13:56:02.890Z","userType":"external","entrypoint":"claude-vscode","cwd":"/Users/edgarpocaterra/ep2-crypto","sessionId":"f48c9af0-2e30-4c92-9024-4c84a03f39db","version":"2.1.81","gitBranch":"main","slug":"spicy-gathering-plum"}
